    Ezekiel

    Tsir 1

    1. Afei ɔbaa dɛ afe a otsia eduasa no mu no, bosoom a otsia anan no mu da a otsia enum no, ber a mowɔ ndɔmmumfo mu wɔ Kebar esutsen ho no, na ɔsorsor buebuei, na muhun Nyankopɔn ho enyido adzehu.
    2. Bosoom no mu da a otsia enum a ɔyɛ ɔhen Jehoiakin no ndɔmmumkɔ afe a otsia enum mu no, , #2 Ahe 24.10-16; 2 Mbe 36.9
    3. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Buzi ba, ɔsɔfo Ezekiel hɔ pɛpɛɛpɛ wɔ Kaldeafo asaase a ɔwɔ Kebar esutsen ho; na EWURADZE ne nsa baa no do wɔ hɔ.
    4. Na mohwɛe, na hwɛ, ehum kɛse bi tui fi kwaamu afamu bae, nsuwusiw kɛse nye gya a ɔabobɔw noho hyɛ mu, na ɔhyerɛn bi etwa no ho ehyia. Na gya no ne finimfin no, biribi a enyi tse dɛ sika na dwetɛ mforae hyerɛn wɔ hɔ.
    5. Na no mu na abɔdze enyikan baanan bi saso fi puei. Na mbrɛ hɔn hwɛbea tse nye yi; wɔwɔ dasanyi ne saso.
    6. Na obiara wɔ enyim anan, na hɔn mu biara wɔ ntsaban anan.
    7. Na hɔn anansa yɛ tromm; na hɔn ananadze tse dɛ nantwiba n'ananadze: na wɔyeyɛɛ hyenhyerɛnn dɛ ayewa a wɔapɔw ho.
    8. Na wɔwɔ nyimpa nsa wɔ hɔn ntsaban ase wɔ hɔn afa anan: na hɔn baanan no wowɔ enyim na hɔn ntsaban dɛm;
    9. hɔn ntsaban toatoa mu; wɔnam a, wonntwa hɔnho; hɔn mu biara nam n'enyim tsenn.
    10. Hɔn enyim ne saso mbrɛ ɔtse nye yi; hɔn baanan no nyina wowɔ nyimpa enyim; wɔ hɔn enyim, na wɔwɔ gyata enyim wɔ enyimfa afamu; wɔwɔ nantwi enyim wɔ abankum afamu; na wɔwɔ ɔkɔr enyim so wɔ hɔn ekyir.
    11. Wɔatserɛw hɔn ntsaban mu hwɛ ɔsor afamu; obiara ne ntsaban ebien ebien toatoa mu, na ebien ebien katakata hɔn nyimpadua ho.
    12. Na hɔn mu biara nam n'enyim tsenn: mbrɛ sunsum rokɔ, na wɔkɔ; wɔnam a wonntwa hɔnho.
    13. Na abɔdze enyikan ne saso dze, hɔn hwɛbea tse dɛ gyabiriw a ɔdzɛw, dɛ mbrɛ ogya atsɛn no hwɛbea tse; ɔkɔ sor ba ase wɔ abɔdze enyikan no ntamu: na gya no dzɛw huoo, na enyinam fi gya no mu.
    14. Na abɔdze enyikan no tutuu mbirika dzii akɔnaaba tse dɛ enyinam ne nyinamee.
    15. Na morohwɛ abɔdze enyikan no, hwɛ, hwiir kor si asaase no do wɔ abɔdze enyikan no nkyɛn, enyim anan no mu biara nedze kor.
    16. Nhwiir no na hɔn nyɛbea tse dɛ sikabereebo enyi: na baanan no nyina hɔn saso kor: na hɔn hwɛbea na nyɛbea tse dɛ hwiir a ɔhyɛ hwiir mu.
    17. Wɔnam a, wɔnam hɔn afa anan no do: wɔnam a, wonntwa hɔnho.
    18. Na hɔn ho nhankra no dze, wɔkrɔn ma ɔyɛ hu; na baanan no nhankra no ayeyɛ enyiwa enyiwa abɔ ho aprɔw.
    19. Na sɛ abɔdze enyikan no rokɔ a, nhwiir no dzi hɔn nkyɛn: na sɛ wɔma abɔdze enyikan no do fi famu a, nhwiir no so mema do.
    20. Beebiara a sunsum no rokɔ no, wɔkɔ; hɔ ara na sunsum no wɔ dɛ ɔkɔ: na nhwiir no mema do wɔ hɔn nkyɛnmu; na abɔdze enyikan no no sunsum wɔ nhwiir no mu.
    21. Sɛ hɔn wɔkɔ a, woyinom so wɔkɔ; na sɛ wogyina a, nna woyinom so woegyina; na sɛ wɔma hɔn do fi famu a, nhwiir no mema do wɔ hɔn nkyɛn: osiandɛ abɔdze enyikan no no sunsum wɔ nhwiir no mu.
    22. Na abɔdze enyikan no n'etsifi wɔ wimu ne saso, ɔtse dɛ ahwehwɛbo a ɔyɛ hu n'enyi, wɔatserɛw mu akatakata hɔn etsifi.
    23. Na hɔn ntsaban tsen tsenn dzi mbɔenyim wɔ wimu no ase: hɔn mu biara wɔ ebien a ɔkata ne nyimpadua afa ha, na hɔn mu biara so wɔ ebien a ɔkata ne nyimpadua afa ha so.
    24. Na sɛ wɔrokɔ a, metse hɔn ntsaban ne dede a ɔtse dɛ esu akɛse dede, ɔtse dɛ Otumfo no ne ndze dede weɔɔ a ɔtse dɛ dɔm ne dede: sɛ wogyina a, wogyaagyaa hɔn ntsaban mu.
    25. Na ndze bi fi wimu a ɔwɔ hɔn etsifi no mu: sɛ wogyina a, wogyaagyaa hɔn ntsaban mu.
    26. Na wimu a ɔwɔ hɔn etsifi no do wɔ ahengua saso wɔ hɔ a ɔtse dɛ hoabo no hwɛbea: na ahengua no ne saso no do na saso a ɔtse dɛ nyimpa a ɔtse do wɔ sor no hwɛbea no wɔ., #Eze 10.1; Nyi 4.2
    27. Na muhun dɛ ɔtse dɛ sika na dwetɛ mforaa enyi, ɔtse dɛ gya a ɔwɔ no mu bɔ no aprɔw no hwɛbea, ɔnam mbrɛ n'asen na mbrɛ ɔdze fa no sor no tse no ntsi; na mbrɛ n'asen na ɔdze fa no ase no no hwɛbea tse no, muhun dɛ ɔtse dɛ ogya, na hyerɛn etwa no ho ehyia.
    28. Dɛ mbrɛ nyankontɔn a ɔwɔ nsuwusiw mu wɔ nsutɔ da mu tse no, mbrɛ ɔhyerɛn a etwa noho ehyia no no hwɛbea tse ara nye no. Iyi nye EWURADZE n'enyimnyam no hwɛbea no ne saso. Na muhunii no, medze m'enyim bɔɔ famu, na metsee obi a ɔrekasa ne ndze.

    Tsir 2

    1. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, gyina wo nan do, ma menye wo nkasa.
    2. Na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ me no, sunsum no bɛhɛɛn mo mu, na ɔmaa migyinaa me nan do; na metsee nyia ɔrekasa kyerɛ me no.
    3. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, Morosoma wo Israelmba nkyɛn, amanaman etuatsewfo a wɔatsew mo do etua no nkyɛn: hɔn na hɔn egyanom afom me, dze ebodu ndɛ da yi ara mpo.
    4. Na mba no yɛ enyiammbɔho na akomadzen; morosoma wo hɔn nkyɛn: na akɛse hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi.
    5. Na hɔn dze, sɛ wotsie o, sɛ woenntsie o, (osiandɛ wɔyɛ etuatsew fi, ) wobohu ara dɛ saa nkɔnhyɛnyi bi aba hɔn mu.
    6. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba dze, mma nnsuro hɔn, eso mma nnsuro hɔn nsɛm, kaansa nkɔkrɔw na nsoɛ wɔ wo nkyɛn, na etse nyankomaketsembowa mu ara mpo a: mma nnsuro hɔn nsɛm, eso mma wo bo nntu wɔ hɔn enyim, kaansa wɔyɛ etuatsew fi mpo a.
    7. Na kɛka me nsɛm kyerɛ hɔn, sɛ wotsie o, sɛ woenntsie o: na wɔyɛ etuatsewfo dodow.
    8. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba dze, tsie dza meka kyerɛ wo yi; mma nnyɛ etuatsewnyi dɛ etuatsew fie no: bue w'anomu, na dzi dza medze rema wo yi.
    9. Na mohwɛe no, nna hwɛ, wɔatsen nsa bi wɔ mo do; na, hwɛ, nwoma mbobɔwee bi wɔ mu;
    10. na ɔtserɛɛw mu wɔ m'enyim; na wɔakyerɛw no mu na n'ekyir: na wɔakyerɛw sukwadwom, na apensi, na mbusu wɔ mu.

    Tsir 3

    1. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, dzi dza ihu no; dzi nwoma mbobɔwee yi, na kɔ, kɛkasa kyerɛ Israel fifo., #Nyi 10.9
    2. Nna mubuee m'anomu, na ɔmaa midzii nwoma mbobɔwee no.
    3. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, dzi nwoma mbobɔwee a medze rema wo yi, na fa hyɛ wo nson ma. Nna midzii; na ne dɛw yɛɛ dɛ ewo wɔ m'anomu.
    4. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, si mu, kɔ Israel fifo nkyɛn, na kɛka me nsɛm yi kyerɛ hɔn.
    5. Na nnyɛ ɔman a hɔn kasaa yɛ ananakasa, na hɔn kasaa yɛ dzen, na wɔasoma wo hɔn nkyɛn, na mbom Israel fifo a;
    6. nnyɛ aman pii a hɔn kasaa yɛ ananakasa, na hɔn kasaa yɛ dzen a enntse hɔn nsɛm ase no bi a. Ampaara sɛ mosomaa wo hɔn nkyɛn a, nkyɛ wobetsie wo.
    7. Na Israel fifo dze, worinntsie wo; osiandɛ worinntsie me; na Israel fifo nyina hɔn momapɔw do ayɛ dzen na hɔn akoma epirim.
    8. Hwɛ, mayɛ w'enyim dzendzen wɔ hɔn enyim, na wo momapɔw do dzendzen wɔ hɔn mmomapɔw do.
    9. Dɛ dɛnkyɛmbo a ɔyɛ dzen sen twerɛbo na mayɛ wo momapɔw: mma nnsuro hɔn, eso mma hɔn enyim nntu wo bo, kaansa wɔyɛ etuatsew fi mpo a.
    10. Bio so ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, me nsɛm a mebɛka akyerɛ wo nyina gye no w'akoma mu, na fa w'asowa tsie.
    11. Na si mu, kɔ ndɔmmumkɔfo no nkyɛn, wo man ne mba no nkyɛn, na kɛkasa kyerɛ hɔn, na se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi; sɛ wobetsie o, sɛ wonnketsie o.
    12. Nna sunsum no maa me do, ma metsee twiradada kɛse bi wɔ m'ekyir, dɛ, Nhyira mfi ne bea do nka EWURADZE n'enyimnyam.
    13. Na metsee abɔdze enyikan no ne ntsaban ne dede ber a wotwutwuuw ho no, na nhwiir a ɔwɔ hɔn nkyɛnmu no ne dede, mekyerɛ twiradada kɛse bi ne dede no a.
    14. Nna sunsum no maa me do, na ɔdze me kɔree: na mokɔr no wenwen mu, wɔ mo sunsum ne hyew mu, na EWURADZE ne nsa yɛɛ dzen wɔ mo do.
    15. Nna mebaa Tel-abib ndɔmmumkɔfo a wɔtsetse esutsen Kebar ho no nkyɛn, na mbrɛ wɔtse no; na medze ahobow tsenaa hɔn mu hɔ ndaesuon.
    16. Na ɔbaa dɛ ndaesuon no wiei no, EWURADZE asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.3.17, Onyimpa ba, mayɛ wo ɔweɔmfo ama Israel fifo: dɛm ntsi tsie m'anomu asɛm, na bɔ hɔn kɔkɔ ma me.
    17. Sɛ mese mumuyɛnyi dɛ, Owu ara na ibowu; na ɔwo ammbɔ no kɔkɔ, na annkasa dɛ erobɔ mumuyɛnyi no kɔkɔ efi n'emumuyɛ kwan no ho, dze agye ne kra nkwa a; mumuyɛnyi kor noara bowu n'emumuyɛ mu; na no bɔgyaa no dze, mobɔhwehwɛ no wɔ wo nsamu.
    18. Naaso sɛ ebɔ mumuyɛnyi no kɔkɔ, na ɔanndan emmfi n'emumuyɛ ho, anaa n'emumuyɛ kwan ho a, obowu noara n'emumuyɛ mu; na ɔwo dze na agye wo kra.
    19. Bio, sɛ tseneneenyi san fi ne ndzeyɛtsenenee ho, na ɔyɛ emumuyɛ, na medze fintsidua to n'enyim a, obowu: osiandɛ ɔwo ammbɔ no kɔkɔ ntsi, obowu no bɔn mu na ne ndzeyɛtsenenee a ɔayɛ no, wɔnnkɛkaa; na no bɔgyaa dze, mobɔhwehwɛ no wɔ wo nsamu.
    20. Naaso sɛ ɔwo ebɔ tseneneenyi kɔkɔ dɛ mma tseneneenyi nnyɛ bɔn, na ɔannyɛ bɔn a, obenya nkwa ara ampa, osiandɛ otsiee kɔkɔbɔ; na ɔwo agye wo kra.
    21. Na EWURADZE nsa baa mo do wɔ hɔ; na ɔsee me dɛ, Soɛr, fir edzi kɔ tɛtɛr no mu, na menye wo nkasa wɔ hɔ.
    22. Nna mosoɛree, na mifiir edzi kɔr tɛtɛr no mu: na, hwɛ, EWURADZE n'enyimnyam gyina hɔ, dɛ enyimnyam a muhunii wɔ esutsen Kebar ho no: na medze m'enyim butuuw famu.
    23. Nna sunsum no bɛhɛɛn mo mu, na ɔdze me gyinaa me nan do; na ɔnye me kasae, na ɔsee me dɛ, Kɔ, kɔtow woho abow mu wɔ wo fie.
    24. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba dze, hwɛ, wɔdze nkyehoma bogu wo do, na wɔdze akyekyer wo, na irimmfir edzi nnkɔ hɔn mu:
    25. na mebɛma wo tɛkyerɛma afam w'anomu, na atɔ mum, na annyɛ kasanyimfo amma hɔn: na wɔyɛ etuatsew fi.
    26. Na sɛ menye wo kasa a, mubobue w'ano, na ase hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Nyia otsie no, ma ontsie; na nyia onntsie no, mma onntsie: na wɔyɛ etuatsew fi.

    Tsir 4

    1. Ɔwo so, onyimpa ba, fa ntaayaa, na fa to w'enyim, na sensan kurow wɔ do, Jerusalɛm a:
    2. na kɔ ho ntuae, na tow ho aban, na hɔr ho pempe; kyer ho nsera so hyia, na fa afasubu ndadzefir sisi ho hyia.
    3. Na ɔwoara fa dadzesɛn, na fa si dadze fasu wɔ ɔwo na kurow no ntamu: na fa w'enyi si do, na wɔbɔkɔ no ntuae, na akɔ no ntuae. Iyi bɛyɛ sɛnkyerɛdze ama Israel fifo.
    4. Bio so, da w'abankum do, na fa Israel fi emumuyɛ to do: nda dodow a ebɛda do no, ebɔsoa hɔn emumuyɛ.
    5. Na mahyɛ hɔn emumuyɛ mfe no dɛ ɔnyɛ nda dodow mma wo, mekyerɛ nda ahaasa eduokron: mbrɛ ebɔsoa Israel fi emumuyɛ nye no.
    6. Na bio, sɛ iwie iyinom yɛ a, da w'enyimfa do, na asoa Juda fi emumuyɛ: adaduanan, da kor afe kor, na mahyɛ ama wo.
    7. Na fa w'enyi si Jerusalɛm ntuae no do, wo nsa ho nda hɔ; na hyɛ nkɔm gu no do.
    8. Na, hwɛ, medze nkyehoma bogu wo do, na irunntwa adafa, dze ekodu dɛ ewie wo ntuae nda no ana.
    9. Na woara fa ewifua pa, na atoko, na eduwa, na asaduwa, na ewifua, na ewi, na fa hyɛ ɔsan kor mu, na fa yɛ edziban; nda dodow a edze bɛda w'afa no, mekyerɛ nda ahaasa eduokron, na ibedzi.
    10. Na w'edziban a ibedzi no ne nkerii bɛyɛ dwetɛbona eduonu da kor: ofi ber to ber na dzi.
    11. Na nom nsu a woesusu no susutoa nkyɛmu esia mu kor: ofi ber to ber na nom.
    12. Na dzi no dɛ atoko tatar, na fa egyanan a ofi nyimpa mu no to hɔn enyim.
    13. Na EWURADZE see dɛ, Dɛmara so na Israelmba bedzi hɔn edziban a ɔyɛ nkɔw, wɔ amanaman a mebɛpam hɔn makɔ hɔ no mu.
    14. Nna mesee dɛ, Ao, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn! Hwɛ, me kra ho nnguu fi: na ofitsi me mbafose besi sesei minndzii dza noara oewu, anaa mbowa atsetse no da; eso nam a wokyir bi nnkɔr m'anomu pɛn.
    15. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Hwɛ, medze nantwibin mahyɛ wo nyimpa efikyir ananmu, na esiesie w'edziban wɔ do.
    16. Bio so, ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, hwɛ, mubobu edziban dua mu wɔ Jerusalɛm: na wobedzi edziban nkerii do, na nhwɛyie mu; na wɔbɔnom nsu nsusui do, na ahobow mu:
    17. ama woeehia edziban na nsu, na hɔn ho abow hɔn, ɔbaako wɔ ɔbaako ho, na wɔaafomfɔn wɔ hɔn emumuyɛ mu.

    Tsir 5

    1. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba, fa afona ndam ndam, dɛ oyifo ne yindam kitsa, na fa twerɛw wo tsir na wo bɔdwesa: na fa nsɛn ker nhwi no, na kyɛ mu.
    2. Fa gya hyew nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor wɔ kurow no finimfin, ber a ntuae nda no ewie du no; na fa nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor so, na fa afona bobɔ ho hyia; na fa nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor so petse mframa mu, na mobɔtwe afona edzi hɔn ekyir.
    3. Na fa mu kumaabi, na fa kyekyer w'atar ano.
    4. Na fa iyinom mu bi bio, na tow gu gya no mu, na hyew no wɔ gya no mu; no mu na gya befir aba Israel fifo nyina mu.
    5. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Jerusalɛm nye yi: medze no esi amanaman finimfin, na nkurow nkurow etwa no ho ehyia.
    6. Na ɔatsew me ntsɛmbu do etua wɔ dɛ ɔayɛ emumuyɛ asen amanaman no, na m'ahyɛdze so do asen nkurow nkurow a etwa no ho ehyia no: na wɔapow m'atsɛmbudze, na m'ahyɛdze dze, wɔannantsew mu.
    7. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Osiandɛ hom yɛ akɔnkyew sen amanaman a etwa hom ho ehyia, na hom annantsew m'ahyɛdze mu, na hom enndzi m'atsɛmbudze do, na hom annyɛ dɛ amanaman a etwa hom ho ehyia no hɔn mmom no.
    8. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hwɛ, emi, emi mara, na menye wo enya; na mubobu atsɛn wɔ wo mu wɔ amanaman enyim.
    9. Na dza mennyɛɛ da no mebɛyɛ no wo mu, na merennyɛ ne saso bio, wɔ w'ekyiwadze nyinara ntsi.
    10. Dɛm ntsi egyanom bedzi mba wɔ wo mu, na mba edzi hɔn egyanom; na mubobu atsɛn wɔ wo mu, na wo nkaase nyina mabɔ apetse mframa nyina mu.
    11. Dɛm ntsi metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, ampaara, osiandɛ edze w'atantandze nyina, na w'ekyiwadze nyina egu mo krɔnkrɔnbea ho fi ntsi, mo so mubokuw wo do; eso m'enyi rennkam do, na mo so murunnhu wo mbɔbɔr.
    12. Wo mu nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor bowuwu yardɔm ano, na ɔkɔm ahyew hɔn wɔ wo mu; na nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor so bɔtotɔ afona ano etwa wo ho ehyia; na nkyɛmu ebiasa mu kor so na mobɔbɔ apetse mframa nyina mu, na matwe afona ataa hɔn do.
    13. Mbrɛ m'ebufuw bowie nye yi, na m'enyiber adwe hɔn do, na mo werɛ akyekye: na wobohu dɛ emi mara EWURADZE na makasa wɔ mo mbɔdzembɔ mu, ber a mewie m'ebufuhyew wɔ hɔn do.
    14. Nkyii so mebɛyɛ wo amamfo na ahorohoraa, wɔ amanaman a woetwa mo ho ehyia no mu, wɔ hɔn a wotwa mu nyina enyim.
    15. Na ɔbɛyɛ ahorohoraa na adapaa, afotu na ahobowdze, ama amanaman a woetwa wo ho ehyia; ber a mubobu atsɛn wɔ wo mu wɔ ebufuw na ebufuhyew, na nkaenyim dzendzen mu no: emi EWURADZE na maka.
    16. Ber a mobɔtotow ɔkɔm mbusu egyen menaba megu hɔn do, dza ɔdze ɔsɛɛ ba a mobɔtotow dɛ medze resɛɛ hom; na mabɛma kɔm adɔɔ hom do so, na mebu w'edziban dua mu;
    17. na mobɔsoma kɔm na mbowa ebusufo aba hom do, na wɔama edzi awo mba ewu; na yardɔm na bɔgya bodua wo mu asen; na medze afona bɛba wo do: emi EWURADZE na maka.

    Tsir 6

    1. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.6.2, Onyimpa ba, ma w'enyi ntsim Israel mbepɔw do, na hyɛ nkɔm kyerɛ hɔn, EZK.6.3, na se dɛ, Hom Israel mbepɔw, hom ntsie EWURADZE Nyankopɔn n'asɛm. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛ mbepɔw na nkokwaa, esuka na mbɔnsa no nye yi: Hwɛ, emi, emi mara, medze afona bɛba hom do, na masɛɛ hom sorɔnsorɔmbea.
    2. Na hom afɔrmbukyia bɛdan afo, na hom ewia ehonyi ebubu: na mobɔtotow hom atɔfoe no egu hom abosom enyim.
    3. Na medze Israelmba hɔn efun bogugu hɔn abosom enyim; na medze hom mbiew apetse hom afɔrmbukyia ho ehyia.
    4. Hom tsenabea nyinara mu nkurow no bɔbobɔ, na sorɔnsorɔmbea no ayɛ afoafo; ama hom afɔrmbukyia eedwurudwuruw, na wɔaayɛ afoafo, na hom abosom eebubu abobɔ adze, na woeetwitwa hom ewia ehonyi no egugu famu, na hom ndwuma no wɔaasɛɛ no.
    5. Na atɔfo no bɔhwehwe ase wɔ hom mu, na hom ehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    6. Naaso mibegyaa nkaase, wɔ dɛ hom benya obinom a wobefi afona nsa wɔ amanaman mu, ber a wɔbɔbɔ hom apetse nkurow nkurow do no.
    7. Na hom mu hɔn a wobefi nsa no wɔbɛkaa me wɔ amanaman a wɔbɔsoa hɔn akɔ hɔ ndɔmmum mu no mu, mbrɛ woedua na wɔdze hɔn ndwamanyɛ akoma a atwe efi mo ho na enyiwa a odzi hɔn abosom ekyir yɛ ndwamandze no egura me: na hɔnankasa hɔn ho bɛyɛ hɔn nkɔw wɔ hɔnankasa hɔn enyiwa do ɔnam mbusu a wɔabɔ wɔ hɔn ekyiwadze nyinara mu no ntsi.
    8. Na wobohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE: nnyɛ gyan ara na maka dɛ mobɔbɔ hɔn mbusu yi.
    9. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Bɔ wo nsamu, na fa w'anan pempem famu, na se dɛ, Ao, osian Israelfi ho ekyiwadze no mbusu ntsi a: na wɔbɔtotɔ afona, kɔm, na yardɔm ano.
    10. Nyia ɔwɔ ekyirekyir no bowu yardɔm ano; na nyia ɔbɛn bɔtɔ afona ano: na nyia ɔbɛka ma wɔakɔ no ntuae no, obowu kɔm ano: mbrɛ mibesi mewie m'ebufuhyew wɔ hɔn do nye no.
    11. Na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, ber a hɔn atɔfoe bɛdeda hɔn abosom ntamu etwa hɔn afɔrmbukyia ho ehyia no, wɔ koko tsentsen biara do wɔ mbepɔw etsifi nyinara, na ndua ebun ebun biara ase, na esudur kusuww biara ase, beebi mbrɛ wɔhyew eduhuam ma hɔn abosom no.
    12. Na mebɛtsen me nsa wɔ hɔn do, na mama asaase no ayɛ afo na ɔabɔ, ofitsi sar a odzi kɔ Dibla afamu no do, wɔ hɔn tsenambea nyinara do; na wobohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.

    Tsir 7

    1. Bio so EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.7.2, Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba, mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se Israel asaase no nye yi, Ewiei nye yi! Ewiei no aba asaase no ne mfɛndzanan no do.
    2. Afei na ewiei no aba wo do, na mobɔsoma m'ebufuw ma ɔaba wo do, na mebu wo atsɛn dɛ mbrɛ w'akwan no tse; na medze w'ekyiwadze nyina bɛba wo do.
    3. Na m'enyiwa rennkam wo do, eso murunnhu mbɔbɔr: na medze w'akwan bɛba wo do, na w'ekyiwadze aka wo mu: Na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    4. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Mbusu bi, mbusu kor pɛ bi; hwɛ, ɔreba.
    5. Ewiei aba, ewiei no aba, ɔasoɛr wo do; hwɛ, ɔreba.
    6. Asaase no do nkorɔfo, w'atsɛmbu aba wo do: ber no edu, da no abɛn; weɔɔweɔɔyɛ da a, na nnyɛ enyigye esebɔ wɔ mbepɔw no do bi a.
    7. Afei ɔrennkyɛr na mehue m'ebufuhyew egu wo do, na mewie m'ebufuw wɔ wo do mebu wo atsɛn dɛ mbrɛ w'akwan tse; na medze w'ekyiwadze nyina aba wo do.
    8. Na m'enyi rennkam, eso murunnhu mbɔbɔr: mobɔtwe w'aso, dɛ mbrɛ w'akwan tse, na w'ekyiwadze aka wo mu; Na hom bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE na mobɔbɔ.
    9. Hwɛ, da no, hwɛ, ɔreba! W'atsɛmbu efir edzi; abaa no abɔ nhyiren, ntsɛn abɔ nkukuduuduw.
    10. Akakabensɛm asoɛr ayɛ emumuyɛ abaa; hɔnara o, hɔn nyimpadodow o, hɔn ahonya o, hɔn mu biara rennka: eso abɔsoyɛ biara rennka hɔn mu.
    11. Ber no aba, da no rotwe bɛn: mma adzetɔnyi nndzi ehurusi, eso mma adzetɔnnyi nndzi nkɔmbɔ: osiandɛ ebufuw aba ne nyimpadodow no nyinara do.
    12. Na adzetɔnnyi rennsan nnkɔ dza wɔatɔn no ho, kaansa wɔda ho tse ase mpo a: na enyido adzehu no ɔfa ne nyimpadodow no nyinara ho, obiara rennsan; eso obiara rennhyɛ noho dzen wɔ ne bra n'emumuyɛ mu.
    13. Wɔabɔ akasamu no mu, na woesiesie adze nyina; naaso obiara nnkɔ ɔsa: osiandɛ m'ebufuw wɔ ne nyimpadodow no nyinara do.
    14. Afona wɔ mfikyir, na yardɔm na kɔm wɔ kurow mu: nyia ɔwɔ haban mu no obowu afona ano; na nyia ɔwɔ kurow mu no, kɔm na yardɔm bɛmen no.
    15. Na sɛ hɔn mu bi fi mu guan a, wobohu hɔn wɔ mbepɔw do, na wɔayɛ dɛ mbɔnsa mu mbubur, hɔn nyinara ridzi awerɛhow, obiara wɔ n'emumuyɛ mu.
    16. Nsa nyinara mu bɔgogow, na anankoroma nyinara ayeyɛ mberɛw dɛ nsu.
    17. Wobofurafura eyitam so, na nketsenketse akyekyer hɔn; na enyim nyinara bogugu ase, na hɔn etsir nyinara do apepa.
    18. Wɔbɔtow hɔn dwetɛ egu abrɔn mu, na hɔn sikakɔkɔɔ ayɛ dɛ efifidze; hɔn dwetɛ na hɔn sika runntum nngye hɔn wɔ EWURADZE n'ebufuw da no mu; wɔnnkɛmee hɔn akra, eso wɔrennhyehyɛ hɔn nson amaama: osiandɛ ɔno na ɔayɛ hɔn emumuyɛ ho fintsidua.
    19. Hɔn ahokadze ne fɛɛfɛw no dze, wɔdze dzii abakombasɛm: na wɔyɛɛ hɔn ekyiwadze na hɔn atantandze no mfonyi no wɔ mu: dɛm ntsi na mama adan hɔn efifidze no.
    20. Na medze bɛhyɛ ananaben nsa dɛ afonam, na asaase no do emumuyɛfo no nsa dɛ asadze; na wobogu ho fi.
    21. Mebɛdan m'enyim so efi hɔn do, na woegu mo sumabea ho fi: na edwotwafo bɛhɛn mu na wobogu ho fi.
    22. Yɛ nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn no: na asaase no do ayɛ ewudzi ma, na kurow no mu ayɛ akakabensɛm ma.
    23. Dɛm ntsi medze amanaman mu abɔn no bɛba, ma wɔabɛfa hɔn efiefi no ayɛ hɔndze: mebɛma ahoɔdzenfo nkontompɔ so abɔ adze; na wobogu hɔn krɔnkrɔn mbea so ho fi.
    24. Sɛ ɔsɛɛ ba a, wɔbɔhwehwɛ asomdwee, naaso wonnkenya bi.
    25. Mbusu bɔbɔ mbusu do, na huhuhuhu abɔ huhuhuhu do; na wɔbɔhwehwɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi hɔ enyido adzehu; na mbra no bɛhera efi asɔfo no ho, na apam efi mpanyimfo no ho.
    26. Ɔhen begyam, na bapɔmba no efura abagura, na asaase no do nkorɔfo no hɔn abaw mu etu: na mebɛyɛ hɔn dɛ mbrɛ hɔn kwan tse, na mebu hɔn atsɛn dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata hɔn; na wobohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.

    Tsir 8

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ afe a otsia esia no mu no, bosoom a otsia esia no mu da a otsia enum no, ber metse me fie na Juda mpanyin no tsetse m'enyim no, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ne nsa tɔɔ mo do wɔ hɔ.
    2. Nna mohwɛe, na muhun nyimpa saso bi a no hwɛbea tse dɛ ogya; na ofi mbrɛ ɔhwɛ dɛ ɔyɛ n'asen na odzi sian no, gya a: na ofi n'asen na ɔdze fow sor no, ɔtse dɛ hyerɛn no hwɛbea, n'enyi tse dɛ sika na dwetɛ mforaforaa.
    3. Na ɔtseen nsa bi ne saso, na osuoo m'etsifi nhwi mu; na sunsum no maa mo do duaa asaase na sor ntamu, wɔ Nyankopɔn enyido adzehu mu dze me baa Jerusalɛm abangua a ɔwɔ mu a ɔhwɛ kwaamu afamu n'abobotsen no ano; mbrɛ nyinkuntwe no honyi a oyi nyinkun no si.
    4. Na, hwɛ, Israel Nyankopɔn n'enyimnyam wɔ hɔ, dɛ mbrɛ hwɛbea a muhunii wɔ tɛtɛr no mu tse no.
    5. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, afei ma w'enyiwa do hwɛ kwaamu afamu. Nna memaa m'enyiwa do mohwɛɛ kwaamu afamu, na hwɛ nyinkuntwe honyi yi wɔ afɔrmbukyia abobokɛse no ano.
    6. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, ana ihu dza wɔreyɛ? Mekyerɛ ekyiwadze akɛse a Israelfo reyɛ no wɔ ha, ma nkyɛ meefi mo krɔnkrɔnbea maakɔ ekyirekyir no? Mbom mbrɛana irubohu ekyiwadze akɛse bi so a.
    7. Na ɔdze me baa abangua abow no ano; na mohwɛe no, na, hwɛ, otokur bi wɔ afasu no mu.
    8. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, afei bɔr fasu no mu: na mobɔɔr fasu no mu no, nna hwɛ, abow nye yi.
    9. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Hɛn mu, kɔhwɛ emumuyɛ ekyiwadze a wɔreyɛ no wɔ hɔ.
    10. Nna mehɛɛn mu kɔhwɛe; na muhun aweaweambowa n'ahorow, na mbowa a wokyir, na Israel fi abosom nyinara a woekrukyekrukye hɔn wɔ afasu no ho ehyia.
    11. Na Israelmba mu mpanyimfo eduosuon gyinagyina hɔn enyim, na Safan ba Jaazania gyina hɔn finimfin, na nyimpa biara ne nsa dze no nduhuamsɛn mu; na eduhuam wusiw no ne nka faa sor.
    12. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, ana ehu dza Israelmba mu mpanyimfo reyɛ wɔ sum mu no, nyimpa biara wɔ n'ehonyi mpia mu, na wɔka dɛ, EWURADZE nnhu hɛn; EWURADZE apa asaase no.
    13. Ɔsee me bio so dɛ, Ebɛda ho ara ehu ekyiwadze akɛse bi so a wɔreyɛ no bio.
    14. Nna ɔdze me baa EWURADZE fie abokɛse no a odzi kwaamu afamu no ano; na, hwɛ, mbaa tsetse hɔ rusu Tammuz.
    15. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, aso ehu iyi? Ibohu ara ehu ekyiwadze akɛse a ɔsen iyinom bio.
    16. Na ɔdze me baa EWURADZE afamu abangua no do, na hwɛ, EWURADZE asɔrdan abow no ano, nkrandaa no na afɔrmbukyia no ntamu, mbarimba bɛyɛ eduonu enum wɔ hɔ a hɔn ekyir dzi EWURADZE asɔrdan no do, na hɔn enyim dzi boka afamu; na wɔkotowee sɔɔr ewia wɔ boka afamu.
    17. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, ana ehu iyi? Aso ɔyɛ adze kakraba ma Judamba dɛ wɔyɛ ekyiwadze a wɔyɛ no wɔ ha yi? Wɔdze akakabensɛm ahyɛ asaase no do ma, na wɔasan ribeyi me ebufuw: na, hwɛ, wɔdze odubaa no ka hɔn hwen.
    18. Dɛm ntsi na mo so mibedzi no ebufuhyew mu: m'enyiwa rennkam do, eso murunnhu mbɔbɔr: na kaansa wɔdze ndze kɛse keka mu gu m'aso mu mpo a, mirinntsie hɔn.

    Tsir 9

    1. Nna ɔdze ndze kɛse kaa mu guu m'asomu, dɛ, Hom mma hɔn a wɔhwɛ kurow no do no wɔntwe mpin, nyimpa biara n'akodze a wɔdze sɛɛ kitsa ne nsamu.
    2. Na hwɛ, mbarimba baasa fi etsifi abokɛse a ɔda kwaamu afamu kwan do no bae, nyimpa biara n'akodze a wɔdze ku kitsa ne nsamu; na barimba baako wɔ hɔn mu a ɔhyɛ ndwera a kyerɛwnyi dubirtoa sɛn ne nkyɛmfamu. Na wɔkɔr mu kegyinaa boran afɔrmbukyia no nkyɛn.
    3. Na Israel Nyankopɔn n'enyimnyam fii kerub a ɔwɔ do no do baa ofi no n'abowano: na ɔfrɛɛ barimba a ɔhyɛ ndwera a kyerɛwnyi dubirtoa sɛn ne nkyɛmfamu no.
    4. Na EWURADZE see no dɛ, Kodua kurow no mu, Jerusalɛm mu, na kɛhyɛ mbarimba a wosi nkrum na wɔkeka mu wɔ ekyiwadze a wɔyɛ no wɔ mu no hɔn momapɔw do nsew.
    5. Na nkaa no so ɔsee hɔn wɔ m'aso mu dɛ, Hom ndzi n'ekyir nkodua kurow no mu, na hom nkuku: mma hom enyiwa nnkam do, eso mma hom nnhu mbɔbɔr:
    6. hom nku akɔdaa, aberantsɛ na ababaawa, na mbofraba na mbaa dwɛɛ: na nyimpa biara a nsewhyɛ wɔ no ho no dze, mma hom mmbɛn no; na hom nhyɛ ase wɔ mo krɔnkrɔn bea hɔ. Nna wɔhyɛɛ ase wɔ atsetsefo a wɔwɔ ofi no enyim no do.
    7. Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom ngu ofi no ho fi, na hom mfa atɔfo nhyehyɛ abangua no do amaama: hom mfir edzi nkɔ. Na wofiir edzi kɔree, na wokunkum no, wɔ kurow no mu.
    8. Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a worukuku no, na aka mo nko no, nna medze m'enyim butuuw famu, na mekaa mu mesee dɛ, Ao, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn! Aso ebɛsɛɛ Israel nkaa nyinara wɔ w'ebufuw a iruhue egu Jerusalɛm do no mu?
    9. Nna ɔsee me dɛ, Israel na Juda fifo emumuyɛ so ntrado, na asaase no do ayɛ bɔgya ma na kurow no mu ayɛ ntɛnkyew ma: na wɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE apa asaase, na EWURADZE nnhu.
    10. Na emi so dze, m'enyiwa rennkam, eso murunnhu mbɔbɔr, na medze hɔn kwan bobua hɔn etsifi.
    11. Na hwɛ, barimba a ɔhyɛ ndwera a dubirtoa sɛn ne nkyɛmfamu no, bɔbɔɔ amandzɛɛ no, dɛ, Mayɛ dɛ mbrɛ ehyɛɛ me no.

    Tsir 10

    1. Nna mohwɛe, na muhun wimu a ɔwɔ kerubfo no etsifi no, na biribi yii noho wɔ do tse dɛ hoabo, no hwɛbea tse dɛ ahengua ne saso.
    2. Na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ nyimpa a ɔhyɛ ndwera no, na ɔsee dɛ, Kɛhɛn ekyinehyia nhwiir no ntamu, kerub no n'ase, na fa gyansenama hyehyɛ wo nsa ebien nyina amaama wɔ kerubfo no ntamu, na petse kurow no do. Na ɔkɛhɛɛn mu wɔ m'enyim.
    3. Afei barimba no kɛhɛɛn mu no, nna kerubfo no gyinagyina dan no ne nkyɛnmu nyimfa afamu; na fua hyɛɛ abangua a ɔwɔ mu no ma.
    4. Nna EWURADZE n'enyimnyam fii kerub no do fowee kɔr sor, na okegyinaa dan no n'abowano; na fua hyɛɛ dan no ma, na EWURADZE n'enyimnyam ne hyerɛn yɛɛ abangua no ma.
    5. Na kerubfo no hɔn ntsaban ne gyegye no wɔtsee no wɔ abowano abangua no do mpo, dɛ Otumfo Nyankopɔn ne ndze, ber a ɔrekasa no.
    6. Na ɔbaa dɛ, ber a ɔhyɛɛ barimba a ɔhyɛ ndwera no, dɛ, Fa gya fi ekyinehyia nhwiir no ntamu, wɔ kerubfo no ntamu no, ɔkɛhɛɛn mu na okegyinaa hwiir no nkyɛn.
    7. Na kerub no tseen ne nsa fii kerubfo no ntamu, ɔdze kɔr gya a ɔwɔ kerubfo ntamu no do, na ɔfaa bi, na ɔdze kitsaa nyia ɔhyɛ ndwera no nsamu, na ɔgyee dze kɔree.
    8. Na nyimpa nsa saso bi puei wɔ kerubfo no ho, wɔ hɔn ntsaban ase.
    9. Na mohwɛe, na hwɛ, nhwiir anan wɔ kerubfo no nkyɛnmu, hwiir kor wɔ kerub kor nkyɛnmu, na hwiir kor so wɔ kerub kor so nkyɛnmu: na nhwiir no hwɛbea tse dɛ sikabereebo enyi.
    10. Na hɔn hwɛbea no dze, anan nyina hɔn saso kor, dɛ gyama hwiir a nkyɛ ɔhyɛ hwiir mu.
    11. Sɛ wɔnam a, wɔnam hɔn afa anan no do: na sɛ wɔnam a, wonntwa hɔnho, na beebi mbrɛ tsir no hwɛ no na wɔka do; wɔnam a, wonntwa hɔnho.
    12. Na hɔn nyimpadua nyina, na hɔn ekyir, na hɔn nsa, na hɔn ntsaban, na hɔn nhwiir no, enyiwaenyiwa ayɛ ho ma etwa ehyia, nhwiir a hɔn baanan no wɔ no a.
    13. Nhwiir no dze, wɔfrɛɛ hɔn wɔ m'asomu, ekyinehyia nhwiir no.
    14. Na obiara n'enyim anan: enyim a odzi kan no yɛ kerub enyim, na enyim a otsia ebien no yɛ nyimpa enyim, na dza otsia ebiasa no yɛ gyata enyim, na dza otsia anan no yɛ ɔkɔr enyim.
    15. Na kerubfo no memaa hɔnho do: iyi nye abɔdze nyikamfo a muhunii wɔ esutsen Kebar ho no.
    16. Na kerubfo no rokɔ a, nhwiir no dzi hɔn nkyɛn: na kerubfo no ma hɔn ntsaban do dɛ wɔrema hɔnho do efi asaase do a, nhwiir no so nndan mmfi hɔn nkyɛn.
    17. Sɛ hɔn wogyina a, nna woyinom so woegyina; na sɛ wɔmema hɔnho do a, nna woyinom so nye hɔn amema hɔnho do: osiandɛ abɔdze nyikan no no sunsum wɔ hɔn mu.
    18. Na EWURADZE n'enyimnyam no fii ofi no abowano kegyinaa kerub no do.
    19. Na kerubfo no memaa hɔn ntsaban do, na wɔmemaa hɔnho do fii asaase do wɔ m'enyim dɛ worifir edzi, na nhwiir no wɔ hɔn nkyɛnmu: na wokegyinaa EWURADZE fie abokɛse a odzi boka no ano; na Israel Nyankopɔn n'enyimnyam no wɔ hɔn etsifi sor.
    20. Iyi nye abɔdze enyikan a muhunii wɔ Israel Nyankopɔn n'ase wɔ esutsen Kebar ho no; na muhun dɛ wɔyɛ kerubfo.
    21. Obiara wɔ enyim anan, na obiara wɔ ntsaban anan; na nyimpa nsa ne saso wɔ hɔn ntsaban no ase.
    22. Na hɔn enyim ne saso dze, enyim a muhunii wɔ esutsen Kebar ho no a, hɔn nhwɛbea na hɔn munantwɛr; hɔn mu obiara nam n'enyim tsenn.

    Tsir 11

    1. Bio so sunsum no maa me do, na ɔdze me baa EWURADZE fie boka afamu abotsen a ɔhwɛ boka no ano: na hwɛ, mbarimba eduonu enum gyinagyina abotsen no ano; na muhun Azzur ba Jaazania na Benaia ba Pelatia, ɔman no mu mbapɔmba no, wɔ hɔn finimfin.
    2. Na ɔsee me dɛ, Onyimpa ba, woyinom nye mbarimba a wɔhyehyɛ emumuyɛ wɔ tsirmu, na wɔma apam bɔn wɔ kurow yi mu:
    3. hɔn a wɔka dɛ, Aber a wɔdze si adan mmbɛnee: kurow yi nye dadzesɛn no, na hɛn nye nam no.
    4. Dɛm ntsi, onyimpa ba, hyɛ nkɔm, hyɛ nkɔm tsia hɔn.
    5. Na EWURADZE no sunsum tɔɔ mo do, na ɔsee me dɛ, Kasa dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Israelmba, mbrɛ hom ase nye yi: na minyim ndzɛmba a aba hom adwen mu.
    6. Hom ama hom atɔfoe adɔɔ so wɔ kurow yi mu, na hom dze n'atɔfoe ahyehyɛ abrɔn no amaama.
    7. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hom atɔfoe a hom dze egugu mu no, hɔn nye nam no, na kurow yi nye dadzesɛn no: na wɔdze hom befi mu efir.
    8. Hom esuro afona no; na medze afona no bɛba hom do, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    9. Na medze hom befi mu efir edzi na medze hom ahyɛ ananaben nsa, na mayɛ m'atsɛmbudze wɔ hom mu.
    10. Hom bɔtotɔ afona ano: mubobu hom atsɛn wɔ Israel he do; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    11. Kurow yi rennyɛ hom dadzesɛn, eso hom rennyɛ nam wɔ mu; mubobu hom atsɛn wɔ Israel he do;
    12. na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE: osiandɛ hom annantsew m'ahyɛdze do, eso hom annyɛ m'atsɛmbudze, mbom hom ekedzi amanaman a etwa hom ho ehyia no hɔn mmom do.
    13. Na ɔbaa dɛ, mehyɛɛ nkɔm no, nna Benaia ba Pelatia wui. Nna medze m'enyim butuuw famu, na medze ndze kɛse mekaa mu dɛ, Ao EWURADZE Nyankopɔn, aso iboku Israel nkaa no ase koraa?
    14. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.11.15, Onyimpa ba, wo nuanom, mekyerɛ wo nuanom, wo bɔgyaa, na Israelfo nyinara, hɔn nyinara, hɔn nye hɔn a Jerusalɛmmba ase hɔn dɛ, Hom mfi EWURADZE nkyɛn nkɔ ekyirekyir; hɛn na wɔdze asaase yi ama hɛn dɛ enyadze:
    15. dɛm ntsi se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Kaansa meyi hɔn akɔ ekyirekyir amanaman mu, na mabɔ hɔn apetse nkurow nkurow mu mpo a, mebɛyɛ hɔn krɔnkrɔn bea mber kakra wɔ nkurow nkurow a wɔakɔ do no do.
    16. Dɛm ntsi se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Mobɔboaboa hom ano efi aman mu, na mapon hom ehyia efi nkurow nkurow a wɔabɔ hom apetse hɔ no do, na medze Israel asaase ama hom.
    17. Na wɔbɛba hɔ na wobeyi no mu atantandze nyina na no mu ekyiwadze nyinara efi hɔ.
    18. Na mebɛma hɔn akoma kor, na medze sunsum fofor ahyɛ hom mu; na mibeyi ɔbo akoma no mefi hɔn honam mu, na mama hɔn honam akoma:
    19. ama wɔaanantsew m'ahyɛdze do, na woedzi mo mmom do, na wɔaayɛ: na wɔbɛyɛ me man, na mayɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn.
    20. Na hɔn a hɔn akoma dzi hɔn atantandze na hɔn ekyiwadze akoma ekyir no dze, medze hɔn akwan bobua hɔn etsifi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    21. Nna kerubfo no memaa hɔn ntsaban do, na nhwiir no dzi hɔn nkyɛnmu; na Israel Nyankopɔn n'enyimnyam wɔ hɔn do wɔ sor.
    22. Na EWURADZE n'enyimnyam fi kurow no ne finimfin foow sor, na okegyinaa bepɔw a ɔda kurow no no boka afamu no no do.
    23. Na sunsum no maa me do, na ɔdze me nam Nyankopɔn no sunsum do kɔr Kaldea ndɔmmumkɔfo no nkyɛn wɔ enyido adzehu mu. Nna enyido adzehu a muhunii no ofii mo do kɔr sor.
    24. Nna mekaa ndzɛmba a EWURADZE dze kyerɛɛ me no nyinara ho asɛm kyerɛɛ ndɔmmumkɔfo no.

    Tsir 12

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ so, dɛ, EZK.12.2, Onyimpa ba, etse etuatsew fi mu; hɔn a wɔwɔ enyi a wɔdze hu, na wonnhu; wɔwɔ aso a wɔdze tse, na wɔnntse; osiandɛ wɔyɛ etuatsew fi., #Isa 6.9
    2. Dɛm ntsi ɔwo, onyimpa ba, siesie tukɔr ndzɛmba na tu ewiaber kɔ wɔ hɔn enyim; na tu fi mbrɛ ewɔ no kɔ beebi fofor wɔ hɔn enyim: bi a wɔbɔdwen ho, kaansa wɔyɛ etuatsew fi mpo a.
    3. Na yi wo ndzɛmba ewiaber fir edzi wɔ hɔn enyim, dɛ tukɔr ndzɛmba: na ɔwoara dze, si mu ewimbir wɔ hɔn enyim, dɛ aber a nkorɔfo rutu akɔ ndɔmmum.
    4. Bɔr fasu mu wɔ hɔn enyim, na soa adze dua mu pue.
    5. Bɔ no akɔnkɔn wɔ hɔn enyim, na fa dua sum mu fir edzi; kata w'enyim mma eennhu daadze: na medze wo mayɛ asɛnkyerɛdze mama Israelmba.
    6. Na meyɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ wɔhyɛɛ me no: medze me ndzɛmba fiir edzi ewiaber, dɛ tukɔr ndzɛmba, na ewimbir no, medze me nsa bɔɔr fasu no mu; medze nam sum mu fiir edzi, na mobɔɔ no akɔnkɔn wɔ hɔn enyim.
    7. Na adze kyee no, EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ dɛ, EZK.12.9, Onyimpa ba, aso Israelmba, etuatsewfo no, nnsee wo dɛ, Ereyɛ dɛn nye yi?
    8. Se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Adzesoa yi fi ɔhen a ɔwɔ Jerusalɛm no ho, na Israelmba nyina a wɔwɔ hɔn mu no ho.
    9. Ka dɛ, Emi nye hom asɛnkyerɛdze: dɛ mbrɛ mayɛ no, dɛmara na wɔdze bɛyɛ hɔn: wobotu akɔ ndɔmmum.
    10. Na ɔhen a ɔwɔ hɔn mu no bɔsoa adze wɔ no kɔn ho wɔ sum mu, na oefir edzi: wɔbɔbɔr fasu mu na wɔdze edua mu efir edzi: ɔbɛkata n'enyim, osiandɛ ɔremmfa n'enyiwa nnhu famu.
    11. Mobɔtow mo boa so megu no do, na wɔapa no wɔ m'efir mu: na medze no bɛba Babilɔn wɔ Kaldeafo asaase do; naaso orunnhu, kaansa hɔ na obowu mpo a.
    12. Na hɔn a woetwa no ho ehyia dɛ wɔbɔboa no nyina, na n'asafo nyina, mobɔbɔ hɔn apetse mframa nyina mu; na mobɔtwe afona no etsiw hɔn.
    13. Na wobohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, ber a mobɔhotse amanaman mu, na mabɔ hɔn apetse nkurow nkurow do.
    14. Na mibegyaa hɔn mu nyimpa kumaabi efi afona, ɔkɔm na yardɔm nsa; ama waaka hɔn ekyiwadze nyina akyerɛ wɔ amanaman a wɔbɛba mu no mu; na wobohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    15. Bio so EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.12.18, Onyimpa ba, fa ahohim dzi w'edziban, na fa ahopopo na nhwɛyie nom wo nsu;
    16. na se asaase no do nkorɔfo no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se wɔ Jerusalɛmmba, na Israel asaase ho nye yi: Wɔdze nhwɛyie bedzi hɔn edziban, na wɔdze ahobow anom hɔn nsu, ama n'asaase ayɛ afo wɔ dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara ho, osian hɔn a wɔtse do nyina hɔn akakabensɛm ntsi.
    17. Na nkurow a wɔtsetse do nyina bɔbɔ, na asaase no adan afo; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    18. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.12.22, Onyimpa ba, ebɛn abɛbusɛm nye yi a hom wowɔ no Israel asaase do dɛ, Nda mu atwe na enyido adzehu biara yɛ kwa yi?
    19. Dɛm ntsi ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Mebɛma abɛbusɛm yi abɔ adze, na worummbu no dɛ bɛ bio wɔ Israel; na se hɔn dɛ, Nda no na enyido adzehu nyina no nsunsuando abɛn.
    20. Na enyido adzehu gyangyan anaa adzɛfɛdzɛfɛw mbusu nkɔnhyɛ biara remmba Israel fi mu ara bio.
    21. Na emi nye EWURADZE; mebɛkasa, na asɛm a mebɛka no, ɔbɛba mu; wɔronntwe nnkɔ ekyir bio: na, etuatsew fi e, hom nda mu na mebɛka asɛm no na mayɛ, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    22. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio dɛ, EZK.12.27, Onyimpa ba, hwɛ, hɔn a wɔwɔ Israel fie no se dɛ, Enyido adzehu a ohu no ayɛ nda pii a ɔreba nedze, na ɔhyɛ mber a ɔwɔ ekyirekyir ho nkɔm.
    23. Dɛm ntsi se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi; Wɔronntwe me nsɛm mu biara nnkɔ ekyir bio, na asɛm a mebɛka no, ɔbɛba mu, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 13

    1. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.13.2, Onyimpa ba, hyɛ Israel nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ nkɔm no do nkɔm, na se hɔn a wofi hɔnankasa hɔn akoma mu hyɛ nkɔm no dɛ, Hom ntsie EWURADZE n'asɛm:
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Ndom nka nkɔnhyɛfo nkwasea a wodzi hɔnankasa hɔn sunsum ekyir na wonnhun hwee no!
    3. Ao Israel, wo nkɔnhyɛfo ayɛ dɛ ekurofo mu nsɔ.
    4. Hom mmfowee nnkɔr ntokur no mu, eso hom nngyee Israel fi ho ban, dɛ wobegyina akono wɔ EWURADZE ne da no mu.
    5. Woehu egyangyandze na ator mbusu nkɔnhyɛ, dɛ wɔka dɛ EWURADZE na ɔse; naaso na EWURADZE nnsomaa hɔn: na wɔama adasa enya enyidado dɛ asɛm no bɛhyɛ ma.
    6. Ana hom nnhun enyido adzehu gyangyan, na hom nnhyɛɛ ator mbusu nkɔm, ber a hom se dɛ, EWURADZE na ɔse; naaso na nnyɛ emi na maka?
    7. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Osiandɛ hom aka nsɛm huhuw na hom ehu ator ntsi, dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, menye hom enya, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    8. Na me nsa bɛda nkɔnhyɛfo a wohu egyangyandze, na wɔhyɛ nkɔntor no do: wɔrommfora me man baguafo mu, eso wɔrennkyerɛw hɔn wɔ Israel fi nkyerɛwee no mu, eso wɔrennhɛn Israel asaase mu, na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE Nyankopɔn.
    9. Osian, osian ara dɛ hom adaadaa me man, dɛ, Asomdwee; na asomdwee biara nnyi hɔ; na sɛ obi tow fasu a, hwɛ, wɔdze kaadow twuw ho ntsi:
    10. se hɔn a wɔdze kaadow twuw ho no dɛ, obobu; nsupramee bɛba; na hom, sorabo akɛse, hom bɔtotɔ; na ehum mframa bɛpaapaa mu.
    11. Hwɛ, sɛ fasu no dwuruw a, ana wɔnnkɛse hom dɛ, Ntwuwho a hom dze etwuw ho no wɔ hen?
    12. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Ehum mframa na medze mebɛpaapaa mu mpo wɔ m'ebufuhyew mu; na nsupramee bɛba wɔ m'ebufuw mu, na sorabo akɛse aba wɔ m'ebufuhyew mu ahyew no.
    13. Nna mubodwuruw fasu a hom dze kaadow etwuw ho no, na medze aka famu, ma ne fapem ho ada hɔ: na obobu, na hom adwerew wɔ mu; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    14. Mbrɛ mubowie m'ebufuhyew wɔ fasu no, na hɔn a wɔdze kaadow twuuw ho no nye no; na mebɛse hom dɛ, Fasu no nye hɔn a wotwuuw ho no nnyi hɔ bio;
    15. mekyerɛ Israel nkɔnhyɛfo no a wɔhyɛ Jerusalɛm ho nkɔm na wohu asomdwee ho enyido adzehu ma no, na asomdwee nnyi hɔ no, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    16. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba, fa w'enyi si wo man ne mbabaa a wofi hɔnankasa hɔn akoma mu hyehyɛ nkɔm no ho; na hyɛ nkɔm gu hɔn do, EZK.13.18, na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Ndom nka mbaa a wɔpempam nsɛbɛ bobɔ hɔn nsakɔn nyina, na wɔyɛ nduukuu ma nyimpa horow hɔn etsir dɛ wɔdze rotwee akra! Aso hom bɔtwee me man hɔn akra, na hom agye akra nkwa ama hom ho?
    17. Na hom egu mo ho fi wɔ me man mu wɔ atoko nsa amaama na boodoo esinesin ntsi, dɛ hom ruku akra a wɔnnsɛ dɛ wowu, na hom dze regye akra a wɔnnsɛ dɛ wɔtsena ase nkwa, ɔnam hom ator a hom dzidzi kyerɛ me man a wotsiee atorsɛm no do.
    18. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hwɛ, Mitsia hom nsɛbɛ a hom dze tweetwee akra wɔ hɔ ma woeetu no, na mebɛtsetsew hɔn mefi hom abaw do; na mebɛma akra no akɔ, mekyerɛ akra a hom tweetwee hɔn ma woeetu no.
    19. Hom nduukuu no so mebɛtsetsew mu na meyi me man efi wo nsamu, mma wɔaannda ho anntsena hom nsamu, mma wɔaanntweetwee hɔn; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    20. Osiandɛ hom dze ator ahow ɔtseneneenyi a emi mara mennhyɛɛ no awerɛhow no no werɛ; na hom ahyɛ mumuyɛnyi ne nsa dzen, amma ɔaannsan emmfi n'emumuyɛ kwan no ho ma wɔaanngye no nkwa:
    21. dɛm ntsi hom runnhu egyangyandze, anaa hom rennhyɛ mbusu nkɔm bio: na mibeyi me man mefi hom nsamu; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.

    Tsir 14

    1. Nna Israel mpanyimfo no bi baa me nkyɛn na wɔtsenatsenaa m'enyim.
    2. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ;
    3. Onyimpa ba, mbarimba yi wɔdze hɔn abosom esuma hɔn akoma mu, na wɔdze hɔn emumuyɛ ne fintsidua esi hɔn enyim: aso ɔsɛ dɛ wɔba mo hɔ ebisa?
    4. Dɛm ntsi kasa kyerɛ hɔn na se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Israel fi mu ɔbarimba biara a ɔdze n'abosom bosuma n'akoma mu, na ɔdze n'emumuyɛ ho fintsidua esi n'enyim, na ɔaba nkɔnhyɛnyi hɔ no; emi EWURADZE mubobua no wɔ mu dɛ mbrɛ n'abosom dodow tse;
    5. ama meesuo Israelmba mu wɔ hɔnara hɔn akoma mu, osiandɛ wɔnam hɔn abosom do atsew hɔnho efi me nkyɛn.
    6. Dɛm ntsi se Israelmba dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hom nsan, na hom ndan hom ho mfi hom abosom ho; na hom ndan hom enyi mfi hom ekyiwadze nyinara ho.
    7. Na Israelmba anaa ahɔho a wɔakɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ Israel no mu obiara a ɔbɛtsew noho efi me nkyɛn na ɔdze n'abosom esuma n'akoma mu, na ɔdze n'emumuyɛ ho fintsidua esi n'enyi do, na ɔaba nkɔnhyɛnyi hɔ ebebisa mo hɔ adze no; emi EWURADZE mara na mubobua no:
    8. na medze m'enyi bɛsa nyimpa no, na mayɛ no ahobowdze ma ɔaayɛ asɛnkyerɛdze na kasabɛbu na mubotwa no efi me man mu akyen; na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    9. Na sɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi bi wɔdaadaa no ma ɔka asɛm bi a, emi EWURADZE na madaadaa nkɔnhyɛnyi no, na mebɛtsen me nsa wɔ no do, na masɛɛ no efi me man Israel mu.
    10. Na wɔbɔsoa hɔn emumuyɛ: nkɔnhyɛnyi n'emumuyɛ bɛyɛ dɛ nyia ɔba no hɔ no n'emumuyɛ no ara;
    11. amma Israelmba aanntɔ gon emmfi me nkyɛn bio, eso wɔaammfa hɔn mbrato eenngu hɔnho fi bio; na mbom ama wɔaayɛ me man na emi so maayɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    12. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.14.13, Onyimpa ba, sɛ asaase bi dze mbrato yɛ me bɔn, na metsen me nsa wɔ no do, na mubu n'edziban dua mu, na mema kɔm ba do, na mutwa nyimpa, na abowa fi do kyen;
    13. kaansa mbarimba baasa yi, Noa, Daniel, na Job, wɔ hɔ mpo a, hɔnara hɔn akra ara na wɔnam hɔn tsenenee do bɛgye, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    14. Sɛ mema mbowa bɔn kyin asaase no do, na wɔsɛɛ no, ma ɔyɛ afo, ma biara nndua do wɔ mbowa ntsi a:
    15. kaansa mbarimba baasa yi wɔ mu a, dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, wɔrenngye mbabanyin anaa mbabaa; hɔnara nko na wɔbɛgye hɔn, na asaase no dze, ɔbɛyɛ afo.
    16. Anaaso sɛ medze afona ba asaase no do, na mese dɛ, Afona e, fa asaase no do ɛ; ma muntwa nyimpa na abowa fi do nkyen;
    17. kaansa mbarimba baasa yi wɔ hɔ mpo a, dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, wɔrenngye mbabanyin anaa mbabaa, na hɔnara nko na wɔbɛgye hɔn.
    18. Anaaso sɛ mosoma yardɔm ba asaase no do, na muhue m'ebufuhyew gu do wɔ bɔgya mu, dɛ murutwa nyimpa na abowa mefi do a:
    19. kaansa Noa, Daniel, na Job wɔ hɔ mpo a, dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, wɔrenngye babanyin anaa babaa; hɔnara hɔn akra ara na wɔnam hɔn tsenenee do bɛgye.
    20. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Na akantam dɛ mobɔsoma m'atsɛmbudze yerɛyerɛw anan, afona, na kɔm, na mbowa bɔn, na yardɔm maba Jerusalɛm do eebotwa nyimpa na abowa efi mu?
    21. Naaso, hwɛ, wobegyaa nkaase bi wɔ mu a wɔdze hɔn befir edzi akɔ, mbabanyin na mbabaa nyina: hwɛ, wobefir edzi aba hom nkyɛn, na hom ehu hɔn abrabɔ na hɔn ndzeyɛɛ: na wɔbɛkyekye hom werɛ wɔ mbusu a medze aba Jerusalɛm do no ho, dza medze aba do nyinara no ho a.
    22. Na wɔbɛkyekye hom werɛ, ber a hom bohu hɔn abrabɔ na hɔn ndzeyɛɛ no: nna hom bohu dɛ dza mayɛ no wɔ mu nyinara nnyɛ kwa ara na mayɛ, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 15

    1. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo ho, dɛ, EZK.15.2, Onyimpa ba, ebɛnadze na wenyindua dze sen dua biara, wenyin abaw a ɔwɔ kwaa mu ndua mu no?
    2. Aso wɔfa no dua bi dze ayɛ edwuma bi? Anaadɛ wɔfa mu bi yɛ bɔfondua a wɔdze adze sɛn do?
    3. Hwɛ, wɔtow kyen gya mu kua no nyena: gya no amen n'ano afa na afa nyina, na ne finimfin no ahyew; aso mfaso bi wɔ ho ma edwuma bi?
    4. Hwɛ, odzi mu no mpo, ɔammfata edwuma biara: na burbur ber a gya no amen no, ma ɔahyew yi, na ɔbɛfata edwuma bi anaa?
    5. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Dɛ mbrɛ wenyindua a ɔwɔ kwaa mu ndua a medze ayɛ nyena ekua gya tse no, dɛmara so na medze Jerusalɛmfo bɛma.
    6. Na medze m'enyi bɛsa hɔn; wobefi gya no mu efir, na gya no bɛmen hɔn; na sɛ medze m'enyi sa hɔn a, hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    7. Na mebɛma asaase no ayɛ afo, osiandɛ wɔato mbra, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 16

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio, dɛ, EZK.16.2, Onyimpa ba, ma Jerusalɛm nhu n'ekyiwadze, EZK.16.3, na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛ Jerusalɛm nye yi: W'awoe na w'awobea wɔ Keenanfo asaase do; w'egya yɛ Amorinyi, na wo na yɛ Hitinyi.
    2. Na w'awobea dze, da a wɔwoo wo no, woenntwa wo funuma, eso wɔammfa nsu ennguar wo ma wo ho emmfir; wɔammfa nkyen ennhura wo ho koraa, eso wɔammfa tam annkyekyer wo ho koraa.
    3. Obiara ne yamu annhyehye no amma wo, annyɛ iyinom amma wo, ammfa ennhu wo mbɔbɔr; mbom wɔtoow wo kyeen sardo prododo, osiandɛ wo nyimpamu yɛ hɔn tan, wɔ da a wɔwoo wo no mu.
    4. Na mubotwaa mu wo nkyɛn, na muhun wo dɛ ereyankam wo bɔgyaa mu no, mesee wo dɛ, Kaansa ewɔ wo bɔgyaa mu mpo a, nya nkwa; nyew, mesee wo dɛ, Kaansa ewɔ wo bɔgyaa mu mpo a, nya nkwa.
    5. Memaa edɔɔr dɛ hamu nkukuduuduw, na ɔwo yɛɛ pii na yɛɛ kɛse, na w'ahoɔfɛw gyinaa mu mbordo; wo mpokuwa bobɔe, na wo tsinhwi fuwii; naaso nna idzi adagyaw na kwatserkwa.
    6. Afei mubotwaa mu wɔ wo nkyɛn, na mohwɛɛ wo no, hwɛ, wo ber no yɛ ɔdɔ ber; na medze m'atarse tserɛɛw wo do, na mekataa w'adagyaw do: nyew, mekaa ntam kyerɛɛ wo, na menye wo dzii ahyɛmu, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, na ebɛyɛɛ medze.
    7. Nna medze nsu guaar wo; nyew, mohohoor wo ho bɔgya koraa fii wo ho, na medze ngo seraa wo.
    8. Mehyɛɛ wo atar a woedzi mu akye so, na mehyɛɛ wo nsukraman nwoma mpaboa, na medze ndwera pa kyekyeer wo ho, na medze serekye kataa wo do.
    9. Medze ahyehyɛdze hyehyɛɛ wo so, na medze nkaba hyɛɛ wo nsa, na medze ntweaban too wo kɔn mu.
    10. Na medze pɛtsea hyɛɛ wo hwen mu, na medze asowamuadze hyehyɛɛ w'asowa mu, na medze abɔtsir fɛɛfɛw bɔɔ wo tsir.
    11. Mbrɛ wɔdze sika na dwetɛ hyehyɛɛ wo nye yi; na wo ntar yɛ ndwera pa, na serekye, na nkyermu, isiam pa na ewo, na ngo, nna idzii: na wo ho yɛɛ fɛw mbordo, na idzii yie kodur ahendzi mu.
    12. Na w'ahoɔfɛw ne nka tahyee kɔr amanaman mu; osiandɛ odzi mu, osian m'enyimnyam a medze mehyɛɛ wo no ntsi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    13. Naaso ɔwo edze wo werɛ tweer w'ahoɔfɛw, na egoor ndwamangor wɔ w'atsenka ntsi, na ihuee wo ndwamangor guu obiara a orutwa mu no do; ɔyɛɛ nedze.
    14. Na ɔwo efaa w'atar bi, na edze yɛɛ nsorɔnsorɔmbea a wɔaka no edur horow maa woho, na egoor do ndwamangor: ndzɛmba a ɔtse dɛm bi nnkɛba, ɔrennyɛ dɛm so.
    15. Ɔwo efaa wo ndwindze fɛɛfɛw, me sika na dwetɛ a medze memaa wo no so bi, na edze yɛɛ mbarimba ehonyi maa woho, na enye hɔn goor ndwamangor;
    16. na efaa wo ntar a woedzi mu akye no dze kataa hɔn do, na edze mo ngo na m'eduhuam sii hɔn enyim.
    17. M'edziban so a medze maa wo no, isiam pa, na ngo, na ewo a medze nyɛɛn wo no, edze sii hɔn enyim mpo dɛ nka huanhuam, nna mbrɛ ɔyɛe nye no; EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    18. Bio so afa wo mbabanyin na wo mbabaa a awo hɔn ama me no, na woyinom na edze hɔn abɔ afɔr ama hɔn dɛ wɔmmemen hɔn. Aso wo ndwamanyɛ yɛ adze ketseaba, EZK.16.21, dɛ ekuku me mba, na eyi hɔn ama, dɛ wondua gya mu mma hɔn?
    19. Na w'ekyiwadze na wo ndwamanyɛ nyinara mu annkaa wo mbofraber mu nda a idzii adagyaw na kwatserkwa, na ereyankayankam wo bɔgyaa mu no.
    20. Na ɔaba dɛ w'emumuyɛ nyinara ekyir no, (ndom, ndom nka wo! EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, )
    21. na atow dampan ama woho, na ayɛ sorɔnsorɔmbea wɔ abrɔn nyinara mu ama woho.
    22. Akwan nyina tsir na ayɛ mpampaa, na ayɛ w'ahoɔfɛw ekyiwadze, na ebue w'anan mu ama obiara a oetwa mu asen no, na ama wo ndwamanyɛ adɔɔ so.
    23. Enye Egyptfo, w'amanyimfo abran no so, agor ndwamangor; na ama wo ndwamanyɛ adɔɔ so dze eyi me ebufuw.
    24. Dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, matsen me nsa wɔ wo do, na mehuan wo daa daa edziban no do, na medze wo ahyɛ hɔn a wokyir wo no hɔn pɛ nsa, Filistiafo mbabaa a hɔn enyi to wo ndwamambra ho no.
    25. Enye Asiriafo so agor ndwamangor, osiandɛ ammee; nyew, enye hɔn agor ndwamangor, naaso ammee.
    26. Nkyii so ama wo ndwamanyɛ adɔɔ so wɔ Keenan asaase do, ekodu Kaldea; na iyiara so mpo ammee wo.
    27. Mbrɛ w'akoma dua yɛ mberɛw a, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, dɛ eyɛ ndzɛmba yinom nyina a ɔyɛ ɔbaa edwaman a oepirim n'enyim ne ndzeyɛɛ;
    28. wɔ dɛ etow wo dampan wɔ akwan nyina tsir, na eyɛ wo sorɔnsorɔmbea wɔ abrɔn nyina mu no; na ɔwo annyɛ dɛ edwaman, wɔ dɛ epow apɛdze.
    29. Ɔyer a ɔto awar! Ɔgye ahɔho hyɛ no kun ananmu!
    30. Wɔkyɛ ndwaman nyinara akyɛdze: naaso ɔwo dze, edze w'akyɛdze mema w'adɔfo nyinara, na ema hɔn mboaba, ama wofi mbeambea nyinara aba wo nkyɛn abɔgor ndwamangor.
    31. Ntsi ɔwo wo ndwamanyɛ no, yɛ soronko fi mbaa binom dze ho, osiandɛ obi ammbɔ wo paa wɔ ndwamangor mu: mbom dɛ ɔwo na ema akatua, na wɔmma wo akatua no, eyɛ soronko ampa.
    32. Dɛm ntsi, edwaman e, tsie EWURADZE n'asɛm:
    33. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Osiandɛ wohuee w'ahonamfi gui, na ɔnam wo ndwamangor a enye w'adɔfo goree ma w'adagyaw daa edzi; na osian w'ekyiwadze abosom no nyinara, na wo mba hɔn bɔgyaa a edze maa hɔn no ntsi;
    34. dɛm ntsi hwɛ, mibehyiahyia w'adɔfo nyinara a enye hɔn agye enyi, na hɔn a ekyir hɔn no nyinara; mobɔboaboa hɔn ano wɔ mbeambea nyina metsia wo, na meyi w'adagyaw edzi makyerɛ hɔn, ma woeehu w'adagyaw nyina.
    35. Na mubobu wo atsɛn, dɛ mbrɛ mbaa a wɔtoto awar ano na wɔka bɔgya gu no wobu hɔn atsɛn; na medze ebufuhyew na nyinkuntwe bɔgyaa bɛba wo do.
    36. Na medze wo bɛhyɛ hɔn nsa so, na w'edwuruw wo dampan na woebubu wo sorɔnsorɔmbea: na wɔbɛpa wo ho efuradze, na wɔafa wo ndwindze fɛɛfɛw no: na wɔbɛdan wo egya adagyaw na kwatserkwa.
    37. Wɔbɔbɔ ngua wɔ wo do so, na woesiw wo abo, na wɔdze hɔn mfona ehwirahwira wo mu.
    38. Na wɔdze gya bɛhyew w'adan, na woebua wo atsɛn wɔ mbaa pii enyim; na mebɛma egyaa ndwamangor, na eremma apɛdze so ara bio.
    39. Nna mebɛma m'ebufuhyew adwe wɔ wo do, na me nyinkuntwe efi wo do, na mayɛ komm, na mo bo rummfuw bio.
    40. Osiandɛ annkaa wo mbofraber mu nda no, na ahow mo werɛ wɔ ndzɛmba yinom nyina mu ntsi; dɛm ntsi hwɛ, mo so medze wo kwan bobua w'etsifi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse: na mma nnyɛ ndwamandze yi mmbɔ w'ekyiwadze nyina do.
    41. Hwɛ, obiara a obubu mbɛ no, obobu bɛ yi etsia wo, dɛ, Mbrɛ na tse no, mbrɛ ne babaa so tse ara nye no.
    42. Wo na ne babaa nye wo, ɔno a okyir no kun na ne mba no, na wo nkyerɛbaa hɔn akyerɛbaa nye wo, hɔn a wokyir hɔn kunnom na hɔn mba no: wo na yɛ Hitinyi, na w'egya yɛ Amorinyi.
    43. Na w'akyerɛbaa panyin nye Samaria a ɔtse w'abankum, ɔno na ne mbabaa: na w'akyerɛbaa kakraba a ɔtse w'abanyimfa no, ɔno nye Sodom na ne mbabaa.
    44. Naaso emmfaa hɔn akwan do, eso ennyɛɛ hɔn ekyiwadze no bi: mbom, mber kakraabi ntamu no, ɔwo esɛɛe seen hɔn wɔ w'akwan nyina mu.
    45. Dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, W'akyerɛbaa Sodom, ɔno na ne mbabaa, ɔnnyɛɛ dza ayɛ yi, ɔwo na wo mbabaa.
    46. Hwɛ, iyi nye w'akyerɛbaa Sodom n'emumuyɛ; ntsɛn, edzidzimee, na ahotɔ dwudwoodwo mu na ɔno na ne mbabaa wɔtsena; eso ɔannhyɛ abɔbɔfo na hianyi nsa dzen.
    47. Na wɔyɛɛ ahopɔw, na wɔyɛɛ ekyiwadze wɔ m'enyim: dɛm ntsi miyiyii hɔn wɔ hɔ dɛ mbrɛ mohwɛ a oye.
    48. Eso Samaria nnyɛɛ wo bɔn mu fa; mbom ɔwo ama w'ekyiwadze adɔɔ so akyɛn hɔn, na edze w'ekyiwadze a ayɛ no nyinara ebu wo nkyerɛbaa bem.
    49. Ɔwoara so, soa woara w'enyito, dɛ ebu atsɛn ama wo nkyerɛbaa; ɔnam wo bɔn a edze ayɛ ekyiwadze asen hɔn no ntsi, hɔn ho tsew sen wo: nyew, ma w'enyim ngu ase so, na soa w'enyito, wɔ dɛ ebu wo nkyerɛbaa bem.
    50. Na medze hɔn ndɔmmumkɔ, Sodom na ne mbabaa hɔn yieyɛ, na Samaria na ne mbabaa hɔn yieyɛ, na wo yieyɛ a wɔwɔ hɔn mu no hɔn yieyɛ bɛsan aba:
    51. ama ɔwoara asoa woara w'enyito, na w'enyi ato wɔ dza ayɛ nyinara ntsi, wɔ dɛ eyɛ akyekyewerɛ ma hɔn no.
    52. Wo nkyerɛbaa, Sodom na ne mbabaa bɛsan aba hɔn asetsena dadaw no mu, na Samaria na ne mbabaa aba hɔn asetsena dadaw no mu, na ɔwo na wo mbabaa bɛsan aba hom asetsena dadaw no mu.
    53. Na wo nkontompɔ da no mu no, ammfa w'ano ammbɔ w'akyerɛbaa Sodom ne dzin;
    54. ansaana woyi w'emumuyɛ edzi no, dɛ ber a Siria mbabaa, na hɔn a woetwa no ho ehyia nyina, Filistiafo mbabaa a woyii wo ehi bɔɔ wɔ aprɔw no, wɔsopaa wo no.
    55. Ɔwo asoa wo ndwamandze na w'ekyiwadze no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    56. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Menye wo bedzi no dɛ mbrɛ ayɛ no ara, ɔwo a ebu ntam no tootooba, edze ato ahyɛmu no.
    57. Naaso emi dze, mebɛkaa m'ahyɛmu a menye wo dzii wɔ wo mbofraber nda no mu no, na mebɛma daa ahyɛmudzi etsim hɔ ama wo.
    58. Ɔno na ebɛkaa w'akwan no, na w'enyi ato, ber a ebɛgye wo nkyerɛbaa, wo nkyerɛbaa mpanyin na nkakraba no: na medze hɔn ayɛ mbabaa ama wo, na ɔnnam w'ahyɛmudzi no do.
    59. Na mebɛma menye wo ahyɛmudzi no egyina; na ibohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE:
    60. ama aakaa, na w'enyim eegu ase, na eemmbue w'ano da biara bio, wɔ w'enyito ntsi; ber a medze dza ayɛ nyinara efir wo no, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 17

    1. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.17.2, Onyimpa ba, ma abrɔme bi, na bu bɛ bi kyerɛ Israelmba;
    2. na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Ɔkɔr kɛse bi, ne ntsaban akɛse akɛse, ne ntsaban ano nsorɔnsorɔmm, ntɛkyerɛ ntokowa ntokowa ayɛ no ho ma, baa Lebanon. Ɔbɛgyee nkyindur ndua etsifi, EZK.17.4, ɔpempaan no nkɔn mu mfefɛwee afor no, na ɔdze kɔr eguadzi asaase bi do; ɔdze kesii eguadzifo kurow bi mu.
    3. Ɔfaa asaase no do aba no so bi, na ɔdze kɛtsɛɛw asaaseber mu; ɔdze sii esu pii ho; ɔtsɛɛw no dɛ esukɔndo dua.
    4. Na onyinii, na ɔbɛyɛɛ wenyindua tantam, na mbom tsiatsiaba a n'abaw tsentsen kɔ no do, na no ndwow wɔ n'ase: nna ɔbɛyɛɛ wenyindua, na ɔtotoo abaw, na ofifiir ahaban.
    5. Ɔkɔr kɛse bi so wɔ hɔ a ne ntsaban akɛse akɛse na ne ntɛkyerɛ pii: na, hwɛ, wenyindua yi fi n'akɔfi do konkoom no ndwow kɔr no do, na ɔtotoo n'abaw kɔr no do, ama oeegugu do.
    6. Wɔtsɛɛw no asaase pa do wɔ esu pii nkyɛn, ama ɔaatoto abaw, na ɔaasow nduadzewa, na ɔaayɛ wenyindua fɛɛfɛw.
    7. Ka dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Aso obowie yie? Aso onnkotutu no ndwow, na oetwitwa no nduadzewa, ama ɔaakyenkyen; ama n'ahaban momon a ɔfefɛw nyina aakyenkyen; dɛ ɔnndze ahoɔdzen kɛse anaa nyimpa pii a wɔdze botutu no efi no ndwow ase.
    8. Nyew, hwɛ, woenya atsɛw yi, aso obowie yie? Aso boka mframa ka no a, ɔnnkɛkyenkyen koraa? Ɔbɛkyenkyen wɔ akɔfi a ofifiir wɔ do no do.
    9. Nkyii so EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.17.12, Afei ka kyerɛ etuatsew fi no dɛ, Aso hom nnyim dza ndzɛmba yinom kyerɛ? Ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Hwɛ, Babilɔnhen baa Jerusalɛm, na ɔbɛfaa no mu hen, na no mu mbapɔmba, na ɔdze hɔn baa ne nkyɛn wɔ Babilɔn;
    10. na ɔfaa adehye no bi, na ɔnye no dzii ahyɛmu; ɔmaa odzii nsew so, na ɔfaa asaase no do akatakyi no kɔree:
    11. ma ahendzi no aabrɛ adze, na ɔaamma noho do, na mbom dɛ obedzi n'ahyɛmu no do na oeegyina.
    12. Na ɔtseew no do etua tutuu ahembɔfo ma wɔkɔr Egypt, ama wɔaama no mpɔnkɔ na nyimpa pii. Aso obowie yie? Aso nyia ɔyɛ ndzɛmba yinom obefi nsa? Aso ɔbɔto ahyɛmu no, naaso oefi nsa?
    13. Dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, ampaara beebi mbrɛ ɔhen a ɔdze no dzii hen a obuu ne ntam enyimtsia, na ɔtoo n'ahyɛmu no ɔtse no, ne nkyɛn hɔ ara wɔ Babilɔn na obowu.
    14. Eso Farao nye no dɔm akatakyi na n'asafo akɛse rinndzi mma no wɔ ɔsa no mu, ber a wɔbɔtotow mpampi na woesisi aban, dɛ wotwitwa nyimpa pii egu.
    15. Osiandɛ oebu ntam no enyimtsia dɛ ɔatoto ahyɛmudzi no ano; na hwɛ, ɔdze ne nsa ama, naaso na ɔayɛ ndzɛmba yinom nyina, onnkefi nsa.
    16. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Dɛ metse ase yi, ampaara me ntam no a oebu no enyimtsia, na m'ahyɛdze no a ɔatoto ano no, medze mubobua noara n'etsifi.
    17. Na medze mo boa mebɛtserɛw no do, na wɔapa no wɔ m'efir mu, na medze no aba Babilɔn, na menye no eyi atsɛn wɔ hɔ wɔ ne mbrato a ɔato etsia me no.
    18. Na n'eguamfo nyinara a wɔwɔ n'asafo asafo mu nyinara bɔtotɔ wɔ afona ano, na hɔn a wɔbɛka no wɔbɔbɔ hɔn apetse mframa nyina mu, na hom bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE mara na maka.
    19. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Mebɛfa nkyindur ndua a ɔkrɔn no nkɔn mu bi so, na medze atsɛw; mebɛpan no nkɔn mu afɔr mfefɛwee fɛɛfɛw no bi, na mara medze akɛtsɛw wɔ bepɔw a ɔwar na ɔkrɔn no no do.
    20. Israel sorɔnsorɔmbea bepɔw no do na mebɛtsɛw no: ama ɔaatoto abaw, na ɔasow nduaba, na ɔayɛ nkyindur ndua fɛɛfɛw. N'ase na nnoma nyina na ntɛkyerɛmbowa nyina bɛgyegye; no ndubaa no nwinwin mu na wɔbɛgyegye.
    21. Na haban mu ndua nyina bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE. Mebrɛ dua tsentsen adze, na mema dua a ɔwɔ famu no krɔn, na mema dua momon kyenkyen, na mema dua wui yɛ prɔmprɔm: emi mara EWURADZE na mase na mebɛyɛ so.

    Tsir 18

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio, dɛ, EZK.18.2, Hom fa no dɛn, na hom bu bɛ yi wɔ Israel asaase ho, dɛ, Egyanom edzi wenyinamba yerɛyerɛw ma mba hɔn se afemfem?
    2. Metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, hom rinnya ho kwan bio ebu bɛ yi wɔ Israel.
    3. Hwɛ, akra nyinara yɛ medze; dɛ mbrɛ egya ne kra yɛ medze no, mbrɛ ɔba so ne kra tse ara nye no: ɔkra a ɔyɛ bɔn no, ɔnoara na obowu.
    4. Na sɛ nyimpa tsen na ɔyɛ dza ɔfa mbra mu na ɔtsen, EZK.18.6, na onndzidzii wɔ mbepɔw no do, eso ɔmmaa n'enyiwa do nnhwɛɛ Israelmba hɔn abosom no, eso onnguu ne nyɛnko ho fi, eso ɔnnkɔr ɔbaa a ɔayɛ bra ho;
    5. eso ɔmmfoom obiara, na mbom ɔdze kafonyi n'ahobadze asan ama no, ɔmmfaa apempensi mmfoom obiara n'adze, ɔdze n'edziban ama nyia ɔkɔm dze no, na ɔdze n'atar ama nyia odzi adagyaw;
    6. nyia ɔmmbɔɔ bosa nnsii akaperɛ, eso ɔnngyee nsiho, ɔatwe ne nsa efi emumuyɛ ho, oebu nyimpa na nyimpa ntamu atsɛn nokwar, EZK.18.9, ɔanantsew m'ahyɛmudzi do, na oedzi m'atsɛmbudze do, dɛ oedzi nokwar a; ɔno na ɔtsen, nkwa ara na obenya, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    7. Sɛ ɔwo babanyin a ɔyɛ odwotwafo, bɔgyakagufo, na ɔyɛ ndzɛmba yinom mu kor biara
    8. na onndzi ndwuma no no mu biara, mbom oedzidzi wɔ mbepɔw no do mpo, na oegu ne nyɛnko ne yer ho fi, EZK.18.12, ɔafom ɔbɔbɔfo na ohianyi, ɔdze apempensi afa obi n'adze, ɔmmfaa ahobadze nnsanee mmae, na ɔama n'enyiwa do ahwɛ abosom, ɔyɛ ekyiwadze, EZK.18.13, ɔabɔ bosa esi akaperɛ, na ɔagye nsiho a: aso obenya nkwa? Onnkenya nkwa. Ɔayɛ ekyiwadze yinom nyinara: owu ara na obowu; no bɔgyaa bogu n'etsifi.
    9. Afei, hwɛ, sɛ ɔwo babanyin a ohu n'egya no bɔn a ɔayɛ nyinara na osuro, na ɔnnyɛ ne saso, EZK.18.15, onndzidzi wɔ mbepɔw no do, eso ɔmma n'enyiwa do nnhwɛ Israel fie abosom, onngu ne nyɛnko ne yer ho fi, EZK.18.16, eso ɔmmfom obiara, ɔnngye biribiara nsi ahoba, eso ɔmmfa apempensi mmfa obi n'adze, mbom ɔdze n'edziban ama nyia ɔkɔm dze no, na ɔdze atar ahyɛ nyia odzi adagyaw, EZK.18.17, ɔatwe ne nsa efi ɔbɔbɔfo ho, onnsi akaperɛ, na ɔnngye nsiho, ɔayɛ m'atsɛmbudze, ɔanantsew m'ahyɛdze do a; orunnwu wɔ n'egya n'emumuyɛ ntsi, nkwa ara na obenya.
    10. Na n'egya dze, susuampaara dɛ ɔayɛ emim, ɔdze apempensi afa no nua afo, na ɔayɛ dza onnye wɔ ɔman no no mu no, hwɛ, obowu wɔ n'emumuyɛ mu.
    11. Naaso hom se dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ɔba nnsoa n'egya n'emumuyɛ? Sɛ ɔba ayɛ dza ɔfa mbra mu na ɔtsen, na oedzi m'ahyɛdze nyinara do, na ɔayɛ a, nkwa ara na obenya.
    12. Ɔkra a ɔyɛ bɔn no, ɔno na obowu: ɔba ronnsoa egya n'emumuyɛ; eso egya ronnsoa ɔba n'emumuyɛ; ɔtseneneenyi ne ndzeyɛtsenenee bɛtsena no do, na omumuyɛnyi n'emumuyɛ atsena no do.
    13. Sɛ omumuyɛnyi san fi ne ndzebɔn a ɔayɛ nyinara ho, na odzi m'ahyɛdze nyinara do, na ɔyɛ dza ɔfa mbra mu na ɔtsen a, nkwa ara na obenya, orunnwu.
    14. Na mbrato a ɔato no mu biara wɔrennkaa nntsia no: ne ndzeyɛtsenenee a ɔayɛ no no mu na ɔbɛtsena ase.
    15. Aso mowɔ enyigye bi wɔ omumuyɛnyi no wu ho? EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse: na nnyɛ dɛ mbom ɔbɛdan efi no kwan mu, na oenya nkwa?
    16. Na sɛ tseneneenyi san fi ne ndzeyɛtsenenee ho, na ɔyɛ emumuyɛ, na ɔyɛ ekyiwadze a omumuyɛnyi yɛ no bi a, aso ɔbɛtsena ase? N'atseneneedze a ɔayɛ no, wɔrennkaa no mu biara: na mbrato a ɔato no mu, na no bɔn a ɔayɛ no mu, ɔnoara mu na obowu.
    17. Naaso hom se dɛ, EWURADZE n'amambu nnsaa. Israelmba e, hom ntsie: Aso m'amambu nnsaa? Ana nnyɛ homara hom amambu na ɔnnsaa?
    18. Sɛ tseneneenyi dan fi ne ndzeyɛtsenenee ho, na ɔyɛ emumuyɛ na owu wɔ mu a; n'emumuyɛ a ɔayɛ no mu na obowu.
    19. Bio so, sɛ omumuyɛnyi dan fi n'emumuyɛ a ɔayɛ no ho, na ɔyɛ dza ɔfa mbra mu na ɔtsen a, ɔbɛgye ne kra nkwa.
    20. Osiandɛ ɔdwendwen ho, na ɔdan fi ne mbrato a ɔato nyinara ho no, nkwa ara na obenya, orunnwu.
    21. Naaso Israel fie se dɛ, EWURADZE n'amambu nnsaa. Ao Israelfo, aso m'amambu nnsaa? Aso nnyɛ homara hom amambu na ɔnnsaa?
    22. Dɛm ntsi, Israel fie, mubobu hom atsɛn, obiara dɛ mbrɛ n'akwan tse, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse. Hom nsan, hom nsan mfi hom mbrato nyinara ho; annyɛ dɛm a emumuyɛ bɛma hom asɛɛ.
    23. Hom ntow hom mbratodze a hom dze ato mbra no nyina mfi hom ho ngu; na hom nya akoma fofor na sunsum fofor mma homho: na ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom bowu, Israel fie?
    24. Na minnyi nyia owu no wu ho enyigye, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse: dɛm ntsi hom nsakyer, na hom nnya nkwa.

    Tsir 19

    1. Na ɔwo dze, ma sukwadwom do wɔ Israel mbapɔmba ho, EZK.19.2, na se dɛ, Mbrɛ wo na si yɛ gyataber: wɔ ngyatanyin ntamu a! Ɔnyɛn ne mba wɔ ngyatafɔr mu.
    2. Na ɔnyɛɛn ne mba no mu kor; ɔbɛyɛɛ gyatafɔr: na osuasuaa ahayɛ, na ɔmemeen nyimpa.
    3. Amanaman so tsee ne nka; wɔkyeer no wɔ hɔn amona mu: na wɔdze nkwaba twee no kɔr Egypt asaase do.
    4. Afei ber a ohun dɛ ɔatweɔn atweɔn, na n'enyidado apa no, nna ɔfaa ne mba no mu baako so, na ɔyɛɛ no gyatafɔr.
    5. Na ɔnantsenantseew ngyata mu, na ɔbɛyɛɛ gyatafɔr: na osuasuaa ahayɛ, ɔmemeen nyimpa.
    6. Na ɔmaa hɔn ekunafo yɛ pii; na ɔbobɔɔ hɔn nkurow, na asaase no, nye dza ɔwɔ mu nyina ho boow hɔn, osian no pɔw ne dede ntsi.
    7. Nna amanaman no fi amantɔw no mu kae kuae botwae yeer no mbea nyinara: na wɔdze hɔn boa tserɛɛw hɔn do; wɔkyeer no wɔ hɔn mona no mu.
    8. Na wɔdze nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn too no na wɔdze no too buw mu, na wɔdze no kɛmaa Babilɔnhen; wɔdze no kɔtoo aban dzendzen mu, amma wɔaanntse ne ndze bio wɔ Israel mbepɔw do.
    9. Nkyɛ wo na tse dɛ wenyindua, wɔ wo bɔgyaa no a wɔtsɛɛw no esu ho: no nsowee na n'abaw yeyɛɛ yie wɔ esu pii no ntsi.
    10. Na onyaa mbaa dzendzen dze yɛɛ nhempoma maa hɔn a wodzi mpanyin, na hɔn tsentsen kɔree kodur nkorbata kusuww no mu, na wohun no no krɔn mu, ɔnye n'abaw no dodow mu.
    11. Naaso wɔpaan no ebufuhyew mu, wɔtoow no kyeen famu, na boka mframa no kyenkyeen no no nsowee no poe: ne mbaa dzendzen no bubui na ɔkyenkyenee: gya no hyeew no.
    12. Na afei wɔatsɛw no wɔ sar do, wɔ asaase kɛsɛɛ a nsu nnyi do no do.
    13. Na gya efi n'abaw no mu, ɔahyew n'abaw na no nsowee, ma abaa a ɔyɛ dzen a wɔdze yɛ ahempoma a wɔdze dzi panyin nnyi no mu hɔ bio. Osukwadwom nye yi, na abɛyɛ osukwadwom.

    Tsir 20

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ afe a otsia esuon no mu, bosoom a otsia enum no, bosoom no ne dadu no, na Israel mpanyimfo no mu bi baa dɛ wɔreba EWURADZE hɔ ebisa, na wɔbɛtsenatsenaa m'enyim.
    2. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.20.3, Onyimpa ba, kasa kyerɛ Israel mpanyimfo, na se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Aso hom aba mo hɔ ebisa? Metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse hom remmba mo hɔ ebisa ara da.
    3. Onyimpa ba, aso ibobu hɔn atsɛn, aso ibobu hɔn atsɛn? Ma wonhu hɔn egyanom hɔn atantandze;
    4. na se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Da a mesaan mu miyii Israel, na memaa me nsa do kyerɛɛ Jakob fi asefo no, na memaa wohun me wɔ Egypt asaase do no, ber a memaa me nsa do kyerɛɛ hɔn, dɛ, Emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn no;
    5. da no na memaa me nsa do kyerɛɛ hɔn dɛ medze hɔn rifir edzi efi Egypt asaase do makɔ asaase bi a makɛsera mahwɛ mama hɔn a numfonsu na ewo pem do a ɔyɛ asaase nyina enyimnyam no no do:
    6. na mesee hɔn dɛ, Hom mu nyimpa biara ntotow n'enyiwa mu atantandze no ngugu, na mma hom mmfa Egypt abosom no nngu homho fi; emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
    7. Na hɔn dze, wɔtseew mo do etua na wɔammpɛ dɛ wotsie emi; hɔn mu nyimpa biara anntow n'enyiwa mu atantandze no enngu, eso wɔammpow Egypt abosom no: nna mesee dɛ mubohue m'ebufuhyew megu hɔn do, medze mewie m'ebufuw wɔ hɔn do wɔ Egypt asaase mu.
    8. Na me dzin ntsi meyɛe mma no ho eenngu fi wɔ amanaman a wɔtse hɔn mu no hɔn enyiwa mu, hɔn a memaa wohun me wɔ hɔn enyiwa mu, dɛ miyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do no.
    9. Dɛm ntsi memaa wofii Egypt asaase do, na medze hɔn mebaa sar no do.
    10. Na medze m'ahyɛdze memaa hɔn, na mekyerɛɛ hɔn m'atsɛmbudze a sɛ dasanyi yɛ a, ɔbɛtsena ase wɔ mu no.
    11. Nkyii so medze m'ahomgyenda so memaa hɔn, ma aayɛ asɛnkyerɛdze ada menye hɔn ntamu, ama woeehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE a metsew hɔn ho no.
    12. Na mbom Israel fifo tseew mo do etua wɔ sar no do: wɔannantsew m'ahyɛdze do, na wɔpoow m'atsɛmbudze a, sɛ ɔdasanyi yɛ a ɔbɛtsena ase wɔ mu no; na woguu m'ahomgyenda no ho fi kɛsenara: nna mesee dɛ mubohue m'ebufuhyew megu hɔn do wɔ sar no do, medze mahyew hɔn.
    13. Na me dzin ntsi meyɛe amma no ho eenngu fi wɔ amanaman a hɔn enyi tuae ma medze hɔn fiir edzi no hɔn enyiwa mu.
    14. Bio so memaa me nsa do wɔ hɔn do wɔ sar no do, dɛ meremmfa hɔn mmba asaase a ɔpem numfonsu na ewo a ɔyɛ asaase nyina enyimnyam a medze memaa hɔn no no do;
    15. osiandɛ wɔpoow m'atsɛmbudze, na wɔannantsew m'ahyɛdze mu, na woegu m'ahomgyenda ho fi: osiandɛ hɔn akoma dzii hɔn abosom ekyir.
    16. Naaso muhun hɔn mbɔbɔr ma mannsɛɛ hɔn, eso mennkum hɔn ase koraa wɔ sar no do.
    17. Na mekaa kyerɛɛ hɔn mba wɔ sar no do, dɛ, Mma hom nnantsew hom egyanom ahyɛdze no mu, eso mma hom nndzi hɔn atsɛmbudze no do, eso mma hom mmfa hɔn abosom nngu homho fi:
    18. emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn; hom nnantsew m'ahyɛdze do, na hom ndzi m'atsɛmbudze do, na hom nyɛ:
    19. na hom nyɛ m'ahomgyenda no krɔnkrɔn na wɔbɛyɛ menye hom ntamu asɛnkyerɛdze, ama hom eehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
    20. Na mba no so tseew mo do etua; wɔannantsew m'ahyɛdze mu, eso woenndzi m'atsɛmbudze no do annyɛ, dza sɛ dasanyi yɛ a, ɔbɛtsena ase wɔ mu no; woguu m'ahomgyenda no ho fi: nna mesee dɛ mubohue m'ebufuhyew megu hɔn do, medze mewie m'ebufuw wɔ hɔn do wɔ sar no no do.
    21. Naaso misiankaa me nsa, na me dzin ntsi meyɛe ma no ho enngu fi wɔ amanaman a medze hɔn fiir edzi wɔ hɔn enyim no enyim.
    22. Nkyii so memaa me nsa do kyerɛɛ hɔn wɔ sar no do, dɛ mobɔbɔ hɔn ahotse amanaman no mu, na mabɔ hɔn apetse nkurow nkurow do;
    23. osiandɛ wɔannyɛ m'atsɛmbudze, mbom wɔpoow m'ahyɛdze, na woguu m'ahomgyenda ho fi na hɔn enyi dzii hɔn egyanom abosom no ekyir.
    24. Nkyii so bio mehyɛɛ hɔn ahyɛdze a onnye, na atsɛmbudze a wɔrenntsena ase wɔ mu;
    25. na muguu hɔn ho fi wɔ hɔnankasa hɔn ayɛyɛdze no mu, wɔ dɛ wɔmaa dza obue wotoa ano nyina oduaa gya mu, ama maasɛɛ hɔnara ma woeehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    26. Dɛm ntsi, onyimpa ba, kasa kyerɛ Israel fifo na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Iyi mu so na hom egyanom akasa mo ho kasa bɔn dɛ wɔato mbra etsia me no.
    27. Na minyae medze hɔn mebaa asaase a memaa me nsa do dɛ medze mebɛma hɔn no no do no, nna hɔn enyi bɔ koko a ɔkrɔn biara, na dɔtɔ wusuww biara do a, nna wɔabɔ hɔ okum afɔr, na hɔ na wɔdze hɔn ehiyi afɔrbɔdze no bae, hɔ ara so na woyii hɔn hua huanhuam, na wɔbɔɔ hɔn ɔnom afɔr wɔ hɔ.
    28. Nna mesee hɔn dɛ, Bea sorɔnsorɔm a hom kɔ hɔ yi, ase nye dɛn? Dɛm ntsi na wɔtoo no dzin Bama araa dze bodu ndɛ da yi.
    29. Dɛm ntsi se Israel fie dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: aso hom egyanom akwan do na hom gu homho fi, na hɔn atantandze ekyir na hom dzi dze gor ndwamangor yi?
    30. Sɛ hom dze hom ayɛyɛdze ba, na hom dze hom mba bɔ ɔhyew afɔr a, hom dze hom abosom nyinara gu homho fi dze bodu ndɛ da yi. Ao Israel fie, aso hom bɛba mo hɔ ebisa? Metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, hom remmba mo hɔ ebisa.
    31. Dza ɔba hom adwen mu no ɔrennyɛ hɔ koraa; wɔ dɛ hom ka dɛ, Yɛbɛyɛ dɛ amanaman no, dɛ nkurow nkurow do ebusua ebusua no na yɛasom dua na ɔbo.
    32. Metse ase yi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, ampaara medze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, na basa a wɔatsen mu, na ebufuhyew a woehue egu mibedzi hom do hen:
    33. na mibeyi hom efi aman mu, na maboaboa hom ano efi nkurow nkurow a mabɔ hom apetse hɔ no mu, medze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, na basa a wɔatsen mu, na ebufuhyew a woehue egu;
    34. na medze hom bɛba aman no hɔn sar no do, na mubobu hom atsɛn wɔ hɔ enyim tua enyim.
    35. Dɛ mbrɛ menye hom egyanom dzii wɔ Egypt asaase sar do no, dɛmara so na menye hom beyi atsɛn, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    36. Na mebɛma hom edua abaa no ase, na medze hom aba ahyɛmu no ne nkyekyeree no mu;
    37. na mibeyiyi hom mu etuatsewfo, na hɔn a wɔto mbra tsia me no; medze hɔn befi asaase a wɔakɛyɛ hɔ no amamforafo no aba, naaso wɔrennhɛn Israel asaase do: na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    38. Na Israel fie, hom dze, mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hom nkɔ, obiara nkɔsom n'abosom ɛ, na n'ekyir no so sɛ hom enntsie me a: na me dzin krɔnkrɔn no dze hom rennda ho mmfa hom ayɛyɛdze na hom abosom nngu ho fi bio.
    39. Na me bepɔw krɔnkrɔn, Israel bepɔw a ɔkrɔn no no do, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse, hɔ na Israel fie nyina, hɔn nyina, wɔbɔsom me wɔ asaase no do: hɔ na wɔbɔsɔ m'enyi, na hɔ na mibebisa hom afɔrbɔdze, na hom ayɛyɛdze mu nduadzewakan no, ɔnye akrɔnkrɔndze nyina.
    40. Hom bɔsɔ m'enyi dɛ hua huanhuam, ber a mibeyi hom efi aman no mu, na maboaboa hom ano mefi nkurow nkurow a wɔabɔ hom apetse do no do; na mo ho bɛtsew wɔ hom mu wɔ amanaman no enyim.
    41. Na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, ber a medze hom bɛba Israel asaase do, kurow a memaa me nsa do dɛ medze bɛma hom egyanom no do.
    42. Na hɔ na hom bɛkaakaa hom abrabɔ, na hom nyɛe nyina a hom dze egu homho fi no; na hom ho bɛyɛ hom nkɔw wɔ hom enyi do wɔ hom mbusu a hom abɔ no nyina ntsi.
    43. Na hom bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, ber a osian me dzin ntsi ma menye hom edzi, na nnyɛ dɛ osian hom akwan bɔn no, na hom ndzeyɛɛ a aprɔw no ntsi, Israel fifo, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    44. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.20.46, Onyimpa ba, fa w'enyi si pomu afamu, na ma w'asɛm nsosɔw pomu afamu, na hyɛ pomu afamu haban no no kwaa no do nkɔm;
    45. na se pomu afamu kwaa no dɛ, Tsie EWURADZE n'asɛm; Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hwɛ, mobɔsɔ gya wɔ wo mu, na ɔbɛhyew wo mu dua momon biara, na dua wui biara: gyaframee a ɔdzɛɛw framfram no orunndum, na ɔbɛhyew enyim nyina fi pomu afamu akɛpem kwaamu afamu.
    46. Na adasa nyina bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE na masɔ; orunndum.
    47. Nna mesee dɛ, Ao EWURADZE Nyankopɔn! Wɔka wɔ mo ho dɛ, Ana nnyɛ mbɛ ara na obubu a?

    Tsir 21

    1. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.21.2, Onyimpa ba, fa w'enyim si Jerusalɛm do na ma w'asɛm nsosɔw ngu krɔnkrɔnbea no do, na hyɛ nkɔm tsia Israel asaase;
    2. na se Israel asaase dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, menye wo enya, na mobɔtwe m'afona efi no bɔha no mu, na metwa atseneneefo na emumuyɛfo efi wo mu.
    3. Ɔnam dɛ mubotwa atseneneefo na emumuyɛfo nyina efi wo mu ntsi na mobɔtwe m'afona efi no bɔha mu no, wɔ adasa nyina do ofi pomu afamu kesi kwaamu afamu;
    4. na adasa nyina bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE na matwe m'afona efi no bɔha mu; ɔrennsan nnkɔ mu bio.
    5. Dɛm ntsi onyimpa ba, si nkrum; fa akoma a ebubu na awerɛhow si nkrum yaayaw wɔ hɔn enyim.
    6. Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ wɔse wo dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na irisi nkrum a? Ɔno se dɛ, Akwansosɛm no ntsi a, osiandɛ ɔreba; na akoma biara bɛnan, na nsa nyina agogow, na sunsum biara atɔ bitsi, na anankoroma nyina ayeyɛ mberɛw dɛ nsu: hwɛ ɔreba, na wɔbɛyɛ, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    7. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.21.9, Onyimpa ba, hyɛ nkɔm, na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Ka dɛ, Afona o, afona o, wɔasew ano, na wɔapɔw ho:
    8. wɔasew ano ama oeekuku; wɔapɔw ho ma ɔaayɛ dɛ enyinam: Yebesi dɛn ama hɛn ho asɛpɛw hɛn? Ebu abaa no enyimtsia, na enyidzi nyina.
    9. Wɔdze afona ama dɛ wɔmpɔw ho, ama wɔdze nsa eesuo mu; afona no, wɔasew ano, nyew, wɔapɔw ho, ama wɔdze aahyɛ okufo nsamu.
    10. Onyimpa ba, Keka mu na bɔ mbubuw: na ɔreba me man na Israel mbapɔmba nyinara do: woeyi hɔn nye me man ama afona: Ao, fa wo nsa hwe wo bo do ae!
    11. Na hwɛ; na sɛ abaa no a obu enyimtsia no mpo nnyi hɔ bio so ɛ? EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    12. Dɛm ntsi ɔwo, onyimpa ba, hyɛ nkɔm, na bɔ wo nsamu; na ma afona no mbra mprɛnu, mprɛnsa, afona a wɔdze dzi ewu a. Afona a odzi ewu kɛse a etwa hom ho nyina ehyia.
    13. Dɛm ntsi hɔn akoma etutu na hɔn a wofintsiw adɔɔ so. Medze afona no n'ano esisi hɔn mbobokɛse nyina ano, Aa! Wɔayɛ no dɛ enyinam; wɔasew ano dze ruboku.
    14. Twa kɔ enyimfa; gyina mpasuar do, kɔ bankum; mbrɛ w'enyi besi biara.
    15. Mo so mobɔbɔ me nsamu na mama m'ebufuhyew adwe: emi EWURADZE na maka.
    16. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio, dɛ, EZK.21.19, Eso onyimpa ba, kyerɛ akwan ebien ma Babilɔnhen no n'afona ndua do mbra; ebien no nyina befir asaase kor do edzi: na sensan bea bi, sensan no wɔ kwan a wɔdze kɔ kurow no mu no ne tsir do.
    17. Kyerɛ kwan a afona no nam do bɛba Ammonmba Rabaa, na Juda a ɔwɔ Jerusalɛm a wɔagye ho ban no mu.
    18. Na Babilɔnhen gyinaa nkwanta do, akwan ebien etsifi, dɛ ɔrehyɛ mbusunkɔm: ɔwosowosoow egyen menaba no, ɔkɔr ebusua honyi hɔ ebisa, ɔhwɛɛ mberɛbo mu.
    19. Jerusalɛm ho mbusu nkɔnhyɛ dze ne nsa nyimfa mu, dɛ wɔmfa afasubu ndadzefir nsisi, dɛ wombue ano wɔ oku mu, dɛ wɔmfa esebɔ mma ndze do, dɛ wɔmfa afasubu ndadzefir a wobesisi mbobokɛse no nsisi, dɛ wɔnhohɔr apempe nsisi, na wɔntotow aban.
    20. Na ɔbɛyɛ dɛ mbusu nkɔnhyɛ gyangyan wɔ hɔn enyi do, ama hɔn a wɔaka ntam egu hɔn do no: na ɔnodze, ɔma wɔkaa hɔn emumuyɛ ama wɔaakyer hɔn.
    21. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Osiandɛ hom ayɛ ma wɔakaa hom emumuyɛ, wɔ dɛ hom mbrato ada edzi, na hom bɔn yi noho wɔ hom nyɛe nyinara mu ntsi; osiandɛ hom aba nkaa mu ntsi, wɔdze nsa bɛkyer hom.
    22. Na ɔwo, omumuyɛnyi otsiɔdzennyi Israelhen ɔwo a wo da edu, ewiei no no mbusu ber no a;
    23. mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Hom nyi akyekyertsir no, na hom mpɔr ahembɔtsir no: ndzɛmba nnkɛyɛ dɛm daa. Ma dza ɔbrɛ adze no do, na brɛ dza ɔkrɔn no adze.
    24. Mubobutuw, mubobutuw, Nyew, mubobutuw no! (Dɛm bi so nnsii da, ) ekodu dɛ nyia ɔyɛ nedze no bɛba; na medze ama no.
    25. Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba, hyɛ nkɔm, na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ka wɔ Ammonmba, na hɔn ahorohoraa no ho nye yi; na se dɛ, Afona, wɔatwe afona, wɔapɔw ho dze ruboku, dɛ ondzi nam, ma ɔaayɛ dɛ enyinam:
    26. ber a wohu egyangyandze ma wo, ber a wɔhyɛ mbusu nkɔntor ma wo, dɛ wɔdze wo bɔto emumuyɛfo etsiɔdzenfo a hɔn da edu wɔ ewiei asotweber mu no hɔn kɔn ho.
    27. Ma ɔnsan nkɛhyɛ no bɔha mu! Beebi mbrɛ wɔbɔɔ wo no, asaase a wɔwoo wo wɔ do no, na mubobu wo atsɛn.
    28. Na mubohue m'ebufuhyew egu wo do; medze m'ebufuw ne gya no mubohuw egu wo do: na mibeyi wo ahyɛ mbarimba etsirmɔdzenfo a wɔawea adzesɛɛ ho hɔn nsa.
    29. Ebɛyɛ nyena ama gya no; wo bɔgyaa bogu asaase no finimfin; wɔrennkaa wo bio: na emi EWURADZE na maka.

    Tsir 22

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio dɛ, EZK.22.2, Na ɔwo, onyimpa ba, aso ibobu atsɛn, aso ibobu bɔgyakafo kurow no atsɛn? Nna ma onhu n'ekyiwadze no nyinara.
    2. Na se dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Kurow a ɔka bɔgya gu wɔ ne finimfin ama ne ber edu, na ɔyɛ abosom tsia noho dze gu noho fi!
    3. Wo bɔgyaa a aka egu no mu na idzi fɔ, na w'abosom a ayɛ no mu na edze egu woho fi; na ama wo nda no abɛn, na edu wo mfe no mpo ho: dɛm ntsi na mayɛ wo enyimguasedze ama amanaman, na atwetwesidze ama nkurow nkurow nyina.
    4. Hɔn a wɔbɛn na hɔn a wɔnye wo ntamu twe besi wo atwetwe, ɔwo a wo dzin asɛɛ na weɔɔweɔɔyɛ ahyɛ wo ma.
    5. Hwɛ, Israel mbapɔmba no, obiara dɛ mbrɛ no tum tse, abɛka bɔgya egu wɔ hom mu.
    6. Wo mu na wɔayeyaw egya na na; wo mu na woedzi ɔhɔho emim: wo mu na wɔafom egyankaba na okunafo., #Eks 20.12; Deut 5.16; Eks 22.21
    7. Ɔwo ebu m'akrɔnkrɔndze enyimtsia, na egu m'ahomgyenda ho fi.
    8. Nkorɔfo a wɔkasa sɛɛ obi dzin no aba hom mu abɛka bɔgya egu: na wo mu na woedzidzi mbepɔw do: wo finimfin na wɔayɛ ndwamandze.
    9. Wo mu na wɔapanta hɔn egyanom adagyaw do: wo mu na wɔabrɛ nyia no ho ekum wɔ n'asabu mu no adze.
    10. Na obi nye ne nyɛnko ne yer ayɛ atantandze; na obi so dze ndwamandze egu n'asew ho fi; na obi so abrɛ n'akyerɛbaa, n'egya ne babaa adze wɔ wo mu.
    11. Wo mu na woedzidzi mboaba dɛ wɔbɛka bɔgya egu; ɔwo esi akaperɛ na agye nsiho, na edze nhyɛdo enya w'amanyimfo ho mfaso edzifodze mu, na wo werɛ efir emi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse., #Eks 23.8; Deut 16.19; Eks 22.25; Lev 25.36
    12. Dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, maprapra me nsamu wɔ w'enyiber mfaso a edzi no ho, na wo bɔgyaa a aba mu no ho.
    13. Aso w'akoma botum sɔw, anaadɛ aso wo nsamu bɛyɛ dzen, wɔ da a menye wo bedzi no? Emi EWURADZE na maka, na mebɛyɛ.
    14. Na mobɔbɔ wo ahotse amanaman mu, na mabɔ wo apetse wɔ nkurow nkurow do; na mebɛhyew wo ho fi mefi wo ho.
    15. Na wo ho bogu fi wɔ amanaman enyim; na ibohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
    16. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.22.18, Onyimpa ba, Israel fi ayɛ dɛ dutu ama me: hɔn nyinara ayɛ boran na kyɛnse na dadze na sumbui, wɔ fononoo mu; wɔyɛ dwetɛfi.
    17. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: Osiandɛ hom nyinara adan dutu ntsi no, dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, mobɔboa hom ano ehyia Jerusalɛm finimfin.
    18. Dɛ mbrɛ wɔboaboa dwetɛ na boran na dadze na sumbui na kyɛnse ano kogu fononoo mu, dɛ wohutsa ho gya mu ma ɔnnan no; dɛmara so na mobɔboa hom ano wɔ m'ebufuw na m'ebufuhyew mu, na medze hom egugu hɔ, na manan hom.
    19. Ampaara, mobɔboa hom ano, na mehutsa hom ho wɔ m'ebufuw gya mu, na hom anan wɔ ne finimfin.
    20. Dɛ mbrɛ wɔnan dwetɛ wɔ fononoo mu no, dɛmara na wɔbɛnan hom wɔ mu; na hom bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE na mehue m'ebufuhyew megu hom do.
    21. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, EZK.22.24, Onyimpa ba, se no dɛ, Eyɛ asaase a wɔnntseew ho, eso nsu nntɔree nnguu do wɔ ebufuhyew da no mu.
    22. No nkɔnhyɛfo tsirdo apam bi wɔ ne finimfin, dɛ gyata a ɔropɔw tsetsew n'afonam mu: wɔamemen akra; wɔfa egyapadze na ndzɛmba a wɔsom bo; wɔama n'ekunafo adɔɔ so wɔ no mu.
    23. N'asɔfoe ayɛ me mbra yerɛyerɛw, na woegu m'akrɔnkrɔndze ho fi: wɔamma sorbi annda dza ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn na dza ɔnnyɛ krɔnkrɔn ntamu, eso wɔamma adasa ennhu he a ɔda dza no ho tsew na dza no ho nntsew ntamu, na wɔdze hɔn enyiwa esuma efi m'ahomgyenda ho, na woegu mo ho fi wɔ hɔn mu.
    24. Hɔn mu mbapɔmba wɔtse dɛ mpataku a wɔropɔw afonam; dɛ wɔbɛka bɔgya egu, na wɔasɛɛ akra, ama woeenya enyiber mfaso edzi.
    25. Na no nkɔnhyɛfo dze kaadow etwuw ho ama hɔn, wohu egyangyandze, na wɔhyɛ mbusu nkɔntor kyerɛ hɔn, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye iyi: naaso na EWURADZE nnkasae.
    26. Ɔman no mu nkorɔfo woedzi emim, na wɔayɛ nwuradandze; nyew, wɔatseetsee bɔbɔnyi na hianyi, na woebu pɛrpɛr do ahaw hɔho.
    27. Na mohwehwɛɛ hɔn mu nyimpa a ɔbɛgye ban no, anaadɛ obegyina tokur mu wɔ m'enyim ama asaase no, amma maannsɛɛ no: na meennhu bi.
    28. Dɛm ntsi mehue m'ebufuhyew megu hɔn do; medze m'ebufuw ne gya mahyew hɔn: medze hɔnankasa hɔn abrabɔ ebua hɔn etsifi, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 23

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ bio, dɛ, EZK.23.2, Onyimpa ba, mbaa beenu, na kor bi mba wɔ hɔ:
    2. na wɔgogoor ndwamangor wɔ Egypt; wɔgogoor ndwamangor wɔ hɔn mbofrabermu: hɔ na womiamiaa hɔn enumfo, na hɔ na wopirapiraa hɔn mbaabun mu mpokuwa.
    3. Na hɔn edzin dze Ohola panyin no, na n'akyerɛbaa Oholiba: na wɔbɛyɛɛ medze, na wɔwoo mbabanyin na mbabaa. Na hɔn edzin no nye yi, Samaria nye Ohola, na Jerusalɛm nye Oholiba.
    4. Na Ohola kɔgoor ndwamangor ber a ɔyɛ medze; na n'enyi hyeew n'adɔfo ho, n'amanyimfo Asiriafo no ho, EZK.23.6, hɔn a wɔhyehyɛ bibir ntar, ambradofo na mpanyin, hɔn nyinara mberantsɛ a hɔn ho yɛ fɛw a, mpɔnkɔdofo a wɔtsetse mpɔnkɔ do.
    5. Na ɔdze no ndwamanyɛ kɔr hɔn do, hɔn nyinara Asiriafo mu mbɛtseefo a: na hɔn mu biara a n'enyi hyeew no ho no, ɔdze hɔn abosom nyina guu no ho fi.
    6. Eso onngyaa no ndwamanyɛ no ofitsi Egypt nda no mu; na ne nkataasiaber mu na wɔnye no dae, na wopiraa ne mbaabun mu mpokuwa: na wohuee hɔn ndwamanyɛ guu no do.
    7. Dɛm ntsi miyii no hyɛɛ n'adɔfo nsa, Asiriafo a n'enyi hyeew hɔn ho no nsa.
    8. Woyinom na woyii n'adagyaw too gua: wɔfaa ne mbabanyin na ne mbabaa, na ɔnoara wɔdze afona kum no: na ɔbɛyɛɛ fen wɔ mbaa mu; na wɔyɛɛ no n'atsɛmbudze.
    9. Na n'akyerɛbaa Oholiba hun iyi, naaso ɔprɔwee wɔ n'enyihyew mu kɛse seen ɔno, na no ndwamanyɛ a ɔdɔɔ so seen n'akyerɛbaa no ndwamanyɛ no mu.
    10. N'enyi hyeew Asiriafo ho, ambradofo na mpanyin, n'amanyimfo a woewuna ntar gɔsɔɔ, mpɔnkɔdofo a wɔtsetse mpɔnkɔ do, hɔn nyinara mberantsɛ a hɔn ho yɛ fɛw a.
    11. Na muhun dɛ no ho egu fi; hɔn beenu no faa kwan kor do.
    12. Na ɔmaa no ndwamanyɛ dɔɔ so; na ohun mbarimba a wɔasensan hɔn mfonyi wɔ fasu ho, Kaldeafo ehonyi a wɔdze edur memen asensan, EZK.23.15, wɔdze abɔdo abobɔ hɔn asen, akyekyertsir a wɔahyɛ no edur sensɛn hɔn etsir ho, ehwɛ hɔn nyina a wɔyɛ dɛ ahenmba, dɛ mbrɛ Babilɔnfo a wɔwɔ hɔn awobea Kaldea no wɔtse no.
    13. Na n'enyi bɔɔ hɔn do ara pɛ na n'enyi hyeew hɔn ho, na ɔsomaa abɔfo kɔr hɔn nkyɛn wɔ Kaldea.
    14. Na Babilɔnfo no baa ne nkyɛn nye no bɛdaa dɔ mpa do, na wɔdze hɔn ndwamanyɛ guu no ho fi, na ɔnye hɔn guu noho fi, na ne kra tseew noho fii hɔn nkyɛn.
    15. Mbrɛ ɔdaa no ndwamanyɛ edzi, na ɔmaa n'adagyaw daa edzi nye no: nna me kra tseew noho fii no ho, dɛ mbrɛ me kra tseew noho fii n'akyerɛbaa ho no.
    16. Naaso ɔmaa no ndwamangor dɔɔ so, dze kaa ne mbofrabermu nda no a ɔgoor ndwamangor wɔ Egypt asaase do no.
    17. Na n'enyi hyeew hɔn mponafo ho, hɔn a hɔn honam tse dɛ nsoasopɔnkɔ honam, na hɔn ahobaa tse dɛ mpɔnkɔ ahobaa.
